# Brivo API

* * *

# Overview

- [Base Urls](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#baseUrls)
- [Authentication](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#authentication)
  - [Headers](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#headers)

    - [Format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#format)

### Base Urls

Brivo accounts can exist in one of two environments. Our base PROD environment corresponds to accounts accessed via access.brivo.com urls. Our EU instance corresponds to accounts accessed via access.eu.brivo.com. Depending on where the account is located you will need to use the following base urls when connecting via API.

##### PROD

| Name | URL |
| --- | --- |
| Auth | https://auth.brivo.com |
| API | https://api.brivo.com |

##### EU

| Name | URL |
| --- | --- |
| Auth | https://auth.eu.brivo.com |
| API | https://api.eu.brivo.com |

### Authentication

The Brivo API uses the OAuth2 3-legged authorization\_code workflow.

Most languages have libraries available for interacting with an OAuth API. In case you are interested in the details we have included a detailed description of how the interaction happens below.
There is a comprehensive list of OAuth Libraries for many languages at http://oauth.net/code/. Internally we use Spring Security Oauth for our Java API clients.

##### Authentication URL's

| Name | URL |
| --- | --- |
| Authentication | {baseURL}/oauth/authorize |
| Token | {baseURL}/oauth/token |

#### Headers

##### Calls to api.brivo.com require a Mashery API key and Authorization header.

| Header | Value |
| --- | --- |
| api-key | API\_KEY |
| Authorization | bearer ACCESS\_TOKEN\_VALUE |

Assigned API Keys can be found in your account on the [developer portal](https://developer.brivo.com/apps/mykeys). Your API Key will need to match the environment that you are trying to connect to. Developer test keys can be generated for PROD via your developer portal login, if you need a test key for EU environments, please contact api@brivo.com.

The Authorization bearer value is the "access-token" returned by the authentication server after a successful authentication.

##### Calls to auth.brivo.com require the following Authorization header.

| Header | Value |
| --- | --- |
| Authorization | Basic CLIENT\_SIGNATURE |

The CLIENT\_SIGNATURE is the base64 encoded concatenation of your CLIENT\_ID:CLIENT\_SECRET with a colon (:) delimeter.

```
For Example:
CLIENT_ID=ABC-123-456
CLIENT_SECRET=qwerty98765

Before Base64 Encode
ABC-123-456:qwerty98765

After encoding
QUJDLTEyMy00NTY6cXdlcnR5OTg3NjU=
```

A Client Id and Secret is obtained by creating an Application in the Brivo sandbox account provided when registering as a developer. Your client credentials must exist in the same environment as the account you are connecting with.

To Create an Application follow these steps:

- Login to Access
- Navigate to Configuration → Integrations
- Click Generate Api Token
- Fill in the Application Name, Application Description, Application Type
- Fill in Redirect URI if using 3-Legged
  - 3-Legged will enabled the authorization\_code grant type and 3-legged OAuth workflow
  - Password will allow you to provide an admin login and password directly, but restricts the application to the owner's account.
- Fill out the form making sure that the redirect\_uri is valid if the 3-legged application type is selected.
- Once created, clicking the Application Details icon will display the Client ID and Secret.

##### Specifying submitted request body content

Any request to api.brivo.com that submits a request body should also include the content-type header field. It is safe to submit this with requests that do not contain a request body as well.

| Header | Value |
| --- | --- |
| Content-type | application/json |

Requests to auth.brivo.com that include body parameters should also include the content-type header field.
For these requests, the request body must be standard form data, and JSON is not supported in the request body.
These content-type header values are supported for auth.brivo.com requests:

| Header | Value |
| --- | --- |
| Content-type | application/x-www-form-urlencoded |
| Content-type | multipart/form-data |

#### OAuth2 Tokens

##### Retrieving a token with the 3-legged OAuth, authorization\_code grant type

###### To start the flow, an authorization request is sent along with the client\_id of the requesting application.

```
GET
https://auth.brivo.com/oauth/authorize

Headers:
Authorization : Basic {BASE64_ENCODED_CLIENT_CREDENTIALS}
api-key       : {api-key obtained from developer.brivo.com}
Content-type  : application/x-www-form-urlencoded

Body:
response_type : code
client_id     : {CLIENT_ID}
state         : {providedState}
```

The state parameter is optional and is generated and tracked by the connecting application.
It will be returned along with the code value to the redirect\_uri so that the application can determine which code response belongs to an initiating request.

The `/oauth/authorize` request will be redirected to the Brivo API login screen which will ask the user to login with their Brivo assigned username and password.

After a successful authentication, a POST request will be sent to the redirect\_uri that was associated with the application at creation time in the Brivo Account Config Tool API Management screens.

The POST request will include a query string value `?code={AUTHORIZATION_CODE}` as well as the `&state={providedState}` value if one was provided with the initial request.

###### Exchange the authorization\_code for an access\_token

```
POST
https://auth.brivo.com/oauth/token

Headers:
Authorization : Basic {BASE64_ENCODED_CLIENT_CREDENTIALS}
api-key       : {api-key obtained from developer.brivo.com}
Content-type  : application/x-www-form-urlencoded

Body:
grant_type    : authorization_code
code          : {AUTH_CODE}
redirect_uri  : {REDIRECT_URI}
client_id     : {CLIENT_ID}
client_secret : {CLIENT_SECRET}
```

The access\_token will be used in the Authorization header to access the Brivo API resources. The token is valid for the duration of the expires\_in value.

##### Retrieving a token with the password grant type

The same headers as mentioned above will still be required

```
POST
https://auth.brivo.com/oauth/token

Headers:
Authorization : Basic {BASE64_ENCODED_CLIENT_CREDENTIALS}
api-key       : {api-key obtained from developer.brivo.com}
Content-type  : application/x-www-form-urlencoded

Body:
grant_type : password
username   : {ADMIN_USERNAME}
password   : {ADMIN_PASSWORD}
```

##### An example token response

```
{
access_token: "[ACCESS_TOKEN_VALUE]",
token_type: "bearer",
refresh_token: "[REFRESH_TOKEN_VALUE]",
expires_in: 60
}
```

After an access token expires, the refresh\_token can be used to request a new access\_token without the need to go through the full authorization\_code workflow until the refresh\_token also expires.

##### Refreshing a token

```
POST
https://auth.brivo.com/oauth/token

Headers:
Authorization : Basic {BASE64_ENCODED_CLIENT_CREDENTIALS}
api-key       : {api-key obtained from developer.brivo.com}
Content-type  : application/x-www-form-urlencoded

Body:
grant_type    : refresh_token
refresh_token : {REFRESH_TOKEN}
```

### Schema

> **Reminder**: When providing data via URL query parameters you must make sure to URL encode them as they may potentially contain characters that are invalid in a URL on their own.

#### Date and Time

##### Format

All date times are represented in the ISO8601 date format to a precision of seconds. Milliseconds are not provided in the response.

```
YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SSZ
```

##### Timezones

All returned datetime values are provided with the UTC timezone.
For example `2015-04-15T12:00:00Z`

Any input time values can specify a desired timezone offset and the api calls will adjust the time values accordingly.
For Example `2015-04-15T17:00:00-05:00`

#### Empty Values

Empty or null values in the domain model are omitted and not transmitted with the json.

In many cases the listing calls will provide a smaller slice of data returned than the retrieval of an individual object.

### Listing Calls

Listing calls are available for most domain groups. Of these, most have optional pagination and filter parameters available to tailor the results as required.

#### Results

The general format for results returned is

```json
{
  "data"     : [ List of domain objects ],
  "offset"   :  Offset from the first result,
  "pageSize" :  Max number of returned results,
  "count"    :  Total number of available results
}
```

#### Paging

Available parameters for result paging ability

##### offset

The offset parameter will start returning results after the specifed offset.
`Default: offset=0`

```
Example:
/users?offset=15
```

##### pageSize

The pageSize parameter specifies the number of results to be returned with the request. The response will provide up to that value.
`Default: pageSize=20``Max : pageSize=100`

```
Example:
/users?pageSize=50
```

#### Filters

The `filter` parameter accepts different filters for each listing call where filtering is available. The general filtering format is:

```
__:
```

- Double underscore `__` is the fieldName and operator separator
- Colon `:` is the separator to the value(s)
- values can be comma separated if a filter allows multiple values
- Multiple filters can be provided using a `;` to separate the filters.

| operator | description |
| --- | --- |
| eq | equals |
| ne | not equals |
| gt | greater than |
| lt | less than |

```
Example:
?filter=id__eq:11,22,33;name__eq:Brivo
```

### Response Codes

#### Success codes

| Response Code | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 200 | Request was successful.<br>If the request was a GET, the response body should have the requested json.<br>If the request for performing some action like an update or create, the response body will generally include an updated domain object. |
| 204 | Successful response where no response body data is returned. Generally returned from a delete operation or after updating an object relationship. |

#### Error codes

| Response Code | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, client Error specifying that invalid request parameters were provided by the requestor.<br>- The response should include details in the request body.<br>- `{ "code" : 400, "message" : "Further details about the BadRequest error response" }` |
| 401 | Unauthorized, An authentication error specifying that no valid credentials or OAuth token were provided <br>- `{"error":"invalid_grant","error_description":"Bad credentials"}`<br>  - Invalid username/password credentials were supplied<br>- `{"status":401,"error":"Unauthorized","message":"Bad credentials","path":"/oauth/token"}`<br>  - An invalid OAuth Basic Authorization token was provided.<br>  - [Check that the included Basic Authorization header is correct](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#headers)<br>- `{"error":"unauthorized","error_description":"Full authentication is required to access this resource"}`<br>  - No Basic authorization header was specified<br>  - [Check that the included Basic Authorization header is correct](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#headers) |
| 403 | Forbidden error, This may be seen <br>- As a response from an end point request where the oauth token is acting on behalf of someone who does not have permission to make the submitted request. This will generally be accompanied by more detailed information in the response body.<br>  - `{ "code" : 403, "message" : "Further details about the Forbidden error response" }`<br>- With a `<h1>Developer Inactive</h1>` response body.<br>  - This indicates that no valid [api-key header](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#headers) was provided. |
| 404 | Not found, provided when a requested object does not exist.<br>- `{ "code" : 404, "message" : "Further details about the not found error response" }` |
| 415 | Unsupported Media Type. Ensure the [content-type header](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#specifying-submitted-request-body-content) is properly set on the request |
| 503 | Service Unavailable, Server side error that may be seen if the API is functioning as expected but a dependent internal service to the request is not available.<br>- `{ "code" : 503, "message" : "Further details about the dependent service being unavailable" }` |
| 596 | Service not found. <br>- `<h1>596 Service Not Found</h1>`<br>- Ensure you are submitting the request with the proper call type (GET, POST, PUT, DELETE) that is specified in the documentation for the endpoint you are calling. |

## Notifications

### TLS 1.0 Deprecation

Brivo will be dropping support for API calls over TLS 1.0 connections on January 31, 2019. To assist you in updating your applications to TLS 1.2+, this document compiles information about TLS and potential user agents that include TLS 1.0 that will need to be updated for your applications to continue to work.

#### Background

Transport Layer Security (TLS) is the protocol used to encrypt HTTPS connections. TLS 1.0 was standardized [almost 20 years ago](https://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2246.txt) as the successor to [SSL 3.0](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc6101), but is vulnerable to attacks such as [BEAST](https://blog.qualys.com/ssllabs/2013/09/10/is-beast-still-a-threat) and [POODLE](https://blog.qualys.com/ssllabs/2014/12/08/poodle-bites-tls).

TLS 1.1 [followed in 2006](https://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc4346.txt) and mitigated BEAST, but major browsers opted to make the [jump directly to TLS 1.2](https://bugzilla.mozilla.org/show_bug.cgi?id=422232#c2) (codified [in 2008](https://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc5246.txt)).

In addition to the documented vulnerabilities, standards bodies such as the [Payment Cards Industry Security Standards Council (PCI SSC)](https://www.pcisecuritystandards.org/) and the [National Institute of Standards and Technology (NIST)](https://www.nist.gov/) recommend disabling TLS 1.0 and TLS 1.1. Specifically, [PCI requires](https://blog.pcisecuritystandards.org/migrating-from-ssl-and-early-tls) that sites use a minimum of TLS 1.1, with TLS 1.2 recommended, and [NIST will require](https://csrc.nist.gov/publications/detail/sp/800-52/rev-2/draft) at least TLS 1.2.

#### Problematic User Agents

Below are the user agents with the highest frequency of TLS 1.0 usage. If your API application is dependent on a user agent in this list, we recommend you consult the documentation provided by the supplier of the service or application for instructions to upgrade your environment as soon as possible.

##### Internet Explorer 10 or Earlier

Internet Explorer did not ship with TLS 1.2 enabled by default until version 11 on Windows 7 and Windows Server 2008 R2. While older versions of IE went [End of Life (EOL) in January 2016](https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/windowsforbusiness/end-of-ie-support), many still exist.

##### Java Runtime Environment (JRE) 1.7 or Earlier

TLS 1.2 support was added to the JRE in [1.7.0\_131-b12](http://www.oracle.com/technetwork/java/javase/7u131-relnotes-3338543.html), so API calls made using older versions of Java may fail.

##### Java 6/7/8

For Java 6 or 7: [Install a new Java Cryptography Extension (JCE)](http://www.ateam-oracle.com/tls-saas-web-services-connections/)

IBM implementations: [Override the default SSL protocol](http://www-01.ibm.com/support/docview.wss?uid=nas8N1022279)

| Java Version | SSL/TLS Default | Other Supported Versions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Java 6 | TLS 1.0 | TLS 1.1 (update 111 and later) |
| Java 7 | TLS 1.0 | TLS 1.2, TLS 1.1 |
| Java 8 | TLS 1.2 | TLS 1.1, TLS 1.0 |

##### Windows OS

[Support for TLS protocols on Windows](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/kaushal/2011/10/02/support-for-ssltls-protocols-on-windows/)
TLS 1.1 & TLS 1.2 are enabled by default on Windows 8.1 releases and afterwards. Prior to that they were disabled by default. Consult Microsoft support for the appropriate Windows version to get the appropriate update to enable TLS 1.1 at a minimum.

| Windows OS Version | TLS 1.0 | TLS 1.1 | TLS 1.2 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Windows XP & Windows Server 2003 | ✓ | X | X |
| Windows Server 2008 \* | ✓ | X | X |
| Windows Vista & Windows Server 2008 SP 2 | ✓ | ✓ | ✓ |
| Windows 7 & Windows Server 2008 R2 | ✓ | ✓ | ✓ |
| Windows 8 & Windows Server 2012 | ✓ | ✓ | ✓ |
| Windows 8.1 & Windows Server 2012 R2 | ✓ | ✓ | ✓ |
| Windows 10 & Windows Server 2016 | ✓ | ✓ | ✓ |

\\* [Update to add support for TLS 1.1 and TLS 1.2 in Windows Server 2008 SP2](https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/4019276/update-to-add-support-for-tls-1-1-and-tls-1-2-in-windows-server-2008-s)

##### .NET Framework

TLS Best Practices for .NET Framework per [Microsoft Docs](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/dotnet/framework/network-programming/tls).

##### PowerShell

[Powershell.org Forum Discussion Regarding TLS 1.2](https://powershell.org/forums/topic/is-it-possible-to-enable-tls-1-2-as-default-in-powershell/)

##### curl

Many developers use [curl](https://curl.haxx.se/) to make API calls. As is common with command-line tools, curl relies on the underlying crypto library that it is built against for SSL/TLS support, e.g., [OpenSSL](https://www.openssl.org/), [NSS](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Mozilla/Projects/NSS), etc. Therefore, users running curl on operating systems with outdated crypto libraries are likely to encounter problems. TLS 1.2 support was first added to OpenSSL in v1.0.1, which was released in March of 2012.

##### Linux OpenSSL

If you are using Linux, you’ll need to know which distribution you are on. You can run cat /etc/\*-release to find this information.

- [Ubuntu](https://help.ubuntu.com/community/OpenSSL)
  - 12.04 LTS (Precise), you will need to take package updates. You can do this by running sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install --only-upgrade openssl, and then restart your application. You may also need to update your libssl. You can update this by running sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get install --only-upgrade libssl-dev.
  - 10.10 (Maverick), 11.04 (Natty), or 11.10 (Oneiric), you will need to upgrade to at least Ubuntu 12.04 (Precise). The easiest way to do this is to rebuild your server, as upgrading from these non-LTS Ubuntu versions is not supported.
  - 10.04 LTS (Lucid), you will need to upgrade to at least Ubuntu 12.04 (Precise). We recommend rebuilding your server, as the upgrade process is risky.

- [RedHat Enterprise Linux, or CentOS](https://access.redhat.com/articles/1462183)
  - Version 6, you will need to take package updates. You can do this by running sudo yum update openssl libcurl, and restarting your application.
  - Version 5, you will need to upgrade to at least Red Hat Enterprise Linux 6.

- Debian
  - You’ll need to use at least Debian 7.0 (Wheezy). The latest OpenSSL version for Squeeze is 0.9.8, when version 1.0.1 is needed. You can use a backport here or upgrade to at least Debian 7.0 (Wheezy).

- Any other Linux variant
  - You will need to ensure that running openssl version gives a version of at least 1.0.1. If it does not, you will need to take package updates, and may need to upgrade to a newer version of your operating system.

##### OS X OpenSSL

If you are using OS X, you can upgrade your OpenSSL version using [Homebrew](https://brew.sh/). You can run brew install openssl to install the latest version of OpenSSL on your machine, then brew install python, brew install ruby, brew install php5, or brew install node to install a Homebrew-managed copy of your language. You will also need to reinstall any dependencies you had already installed.

##### Windows OpenSSL

If you are using a Windows machine, your development environment is providing your copy of OpenSSL. You can upgrade this by upgrading your development environment itself, i.e. your installation of [Python](https://python-security.readthedocs.io/ssl.html#openssl-versions), [Ruby](https://bundler.io/v1.16/guides/rubygems_tls_ssl_troubleshooting_guide.html#windows-installed-with-ruby-installer), [PHP](http://php.net/manual/en/openssl.installation.php), or [Node](https://nodejs.org/en/).

_Please contact [BrivoApi@Brivo.com](mailto:BrivoApi@Brivo.com) with any questions or concerns about these changes._

# Access Point

# Access\_Point - Access Point Activation

Unlocks an Access Point at the Administrators request.

- Administrator must have permission to unlock the access-point
- Access Point must be enabled for activation.
  - To enable or disabled activation navigate to the related Door in Account Config Tool and check the Control From Browser field.

For the most common use case this results in a Door opening. Only Access Points which have an Activation Enabled value of true can be activated via the api. To enable this navigate to a Door in Account Config Tool and check the Control From Browser field.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/access-points/{accessPointId}/activate
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| accessPointId | number | The id associated with the accesspoint |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Access_Point-ActivateAccessPoint-0_0_0-0)

```text
HTTP/1.1 200 Success
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 404 | Not Found, the access point specified does not exist or is not accessible |
| 412 | Precondition failed, the specified access point is not connected |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-ActivateAccessPoint-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-ActivateAccessPoint-0_0_0-1)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-ActivateAccessPoint-0_0_0-2)
- [412 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-ActivateAccessPoint-0_0_0-3)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
    "code": 404,
    "message": "Unknown Access Point"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 412 Service unavailable
{
  "code"    : 412,
  "message" : "Access point is not connected"
}
```

# Access\_Point - Access Point Listing

Retrieve a listing of access points which the current user has view permissions for.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/access-points
```

- [Filter-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#examples-Access_Point-ListAccessPoints-0_0_0-0)

```text
/access-points?filter=name__eq:door1
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | Number | The count of where to start the requested Page<br>Default value: `0` |
| pageSize optional | Number | The number of records to return in a Page, default size is 20 and max size is 100.<br>Default value: `20`<br>Size range: `1-100` |
| filter optional | text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are<br>- `name`<br>  - Filters based on an access point's name<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any access point with a name that contains the provided name value<br>- `report_live_status`<br>  - Filters based on live status value<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: "true" includes any access point where the live status is true. "false" includes any access points where the live status is null or false. NOTE: Live status is only supported for 6k and 300 panels. |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | AccessPoint\[\] | Listing of Access Point Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |
| count | Number | Total count of results available for criteria |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Access_Point-ListAccessPoints-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
 "offset"  : 0,
 "pageSize": 20,
 "count"   : 2,
 "data"    : [{\
                "id"                : 111111,\
                "name"              : "Front door",\
                "controlPanelId"    : 1111,\
                "siteId"            : 11111,\
                "siteName"          : "Site 1",\
                "activationEnabled" : true,\
                "twoFactorEnabled"  : true\
              }]
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-ListAccessPoints-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

# Access\_Point - Access Point Retrieval

Retrieve an Access Point based on the id.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/access-points/{accessPointId}
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| accessPointId | number | The id associated with the accesspoint |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id associated with the access point |
| name | Text | The access point's name |
| controlPanelId | Number | The id associated with the control panel access point is on |
| siteId | Number | The id associated with the site access point is on |
| siteName | Text | The site's name |
| activationEnabled | Boolean | Whether or not the access point has activation enabled |
| twoFactorEnabled | Boolean | Whether or not the access point supports two-factor |
| unlockScheduleId | Number | Displays the access points associated unlock schedule id if there is one |
| unlockScheduleName | Text | Displays the access points associated unlock schedule name if there is one |
| unlockScheduleEnablingGroupId | Number | Displays the access points associated unlock schedule id enabling group id if there is one |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Access_Point-GetAccessPoint-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "id"                : 111111,
  "name"              : "Front door",
  "controlPanelId"    : 1111,
  "siteId"            : 11111,
  "siteName"          : "Site 1",
  "activationEnabled" : true,
  "twoFactorEnabled"  : true,
  "unlockScheduleId"  : 333333,
  "unlockScheduleName": "9 to 5 Schedule",
  "unlockScheduleEnablingGroupId" : 555555
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 404 | Not Found, the access point specified does not exist or is not accessible |

- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-GetAccessPoint-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
    "code": 404,
    "message": "Unknown Access Point"
}
```

# Access\_Point - Door Override Cancel

Cancels an override to the Schedule State of an access point.

- After successfully canceling an override, this endpoint will wait up to 10 seconds to retrieve the updated access point status after setting a door override, at which point the response will include the value of `accessPointState` as `UNKNOWN`. The most recent status can be retrieved using the [Access Point Live Status](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#api-Access_Point-Live_Status) endpoint.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/schedules/change-state/{accessPointId}
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| accessPointId | Number | The id associated with the access point |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| accessPointName | Text | The name of this access point |
| accessPointState | Text |  |
| accessPointScheduledState | Text | The current base lock/unlock state of the access point, taking into account any schedule, schedule override, and threat level applied; as of the time specified in the `statusUpdated` field. The door input status is NOT reflected in this value, but is reflected in the `accessPointInputState` Value may be `LOCK` or `UNLOCK`, or `UNKNOWN` in the event that the access point's state could not be retrieved or has not yet been set. |
| accessPointInputState | Text | The actual status of the access point according to the door input relay, which takes into account whether the door has been unlocked (e.g. via an admin pulse or presenting a credential) in addition to the scheduled unlock state. |
| statusUpdated optional | DateTime | The timestamp for when the `accessPointState` was retrieved. This field is not included if the state is unknown. |
| siteName | Text | The name of the access point's site |
| siteTimezone | Text | The name of the time zone for this access point's site |
| panelName | Text | The name of this access point's control panel |
| panelCpNumber | Text | The CP number of this access point's control panel |
| canPanelSupportScheduleOverride | Boolean | Whether or not this control panel can support door override. Door Override is supported by ACS100, ACS300, ACS6000 and ACS-SDC panels with firmware version 6.1.4 or higher. |
| unlockSchedule optional | UnlockSchedule | Describes the access point's unlock schedule, if one is configured. |
| scheduleOverride optional | DoorOverride | Describes the access point's current door override, if one is in effect. |

## UnlockSchedule

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The ID of the unlock schedule |
| name | Text | The name of the unlock schedule |
| isScheduleBlockActive | Boolean | Whether this unlock schedule is currently active. If the access point is scheduled to be unlocked, this will be `true`. |
| nextTimeChange | DateTime | The next time that this unlock schedule will change state. |

## DoorOverride

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| endTimeMode | Text | The end time mode of the override. Possible values are:<br>- `UNTIL_TIME`<br>  - The override will stay in effect until a specified time.<br>- `UNTIL_NEXT_SCHEDULE_CHANGE`<br>  - The override will stay in effect until the next time the access point's associated unlock schedule change occurs.<br>- `INDEFINITE`<br>  - The override will stay in effect until it is manually removed. |
| behavior | Text | Whether the override is to lock or unlock the access point. Possible values are `LOCK` and `UNLOCK`. |
| endTime optional | DateTime | The time at which the override will end. Not present when `endTimeMode` is `INDEFINITE`. |

- [Success-Response](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Access_Point-Door_Override_Cancel-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "accessPointName": "Front Door",
    "accessPointState": "UNLOCKED",
    "statusUpdated": "2020-04-17T18:23:52Z"
    "siteName": "HQ Site",
    "siteTimezone": "US/Eastern",
    "panelName": "Panel THB-XJ-YYBIR",
    "panelCpNumber": "THB-XJ-YYBIR",
    "canPanelSupportScheduleOverride": true,
    "unlockSchedule": {
        "id": 1111,
        "name": "9-5 Monday-Friday",
        "isScheduleBlockActive": true,
        "nextTimeChange": "2020-04-17T21:00:00Z"
    },
    "scheduleOverride": {
        "endTimeMode": "UNTIL_TIME",
        "behavior": "UNLOCK",
        "endTime": "2020-04-18T00:00:00Z"
    }
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 404 | Not Found, the access point specified does not exist or is not accessible |
| 412 | Precondition failed, the access point does not support overrides or there is not currently one in effect |
| 417 | Expectation failed, canceling the override failed due to an offline control panel or network communication error |

- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-Door_Override_Cancel-0_0_0-0)
- [412 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-Door_Override_Cancel-0_0_0-1)
- [417 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-Door_Override_Cancel-0_0_0-2)

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
    "code": 404,
    "message": "Unknown Access Point"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 412 Precondition Failed
{
    "code": 412,
    "message": "This door does not have a schedule override"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 417 Expectation Failed
{
    "code": 417,
    "message": "Could not reach device to cancel your schedule override."
}
```

# Access\_Point - Door Override

Temporarily overrides the Schedule State of an access point

- This override takes precedence over schedules, holidays, and schedule exceptions, but not lockdown.
- While an override is in effect, administrators will not be unable to change the access point's unlock schedule or edit the schedule itself.
- An access point may only have one override at a time.
- If live status reporting is not yet enabled for this access point, it will be enabled.
- After successfully setting an override, this endpoint will wait up to 10 seconds to retrieve the updated access point status after setting a door override, at which point the response will include the value of `accessPointState` as `UNKNOWN`. The most recent status can be retrieved using the [Access Point Live Status](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#api-Access_Point-Live_Status) endpoint.
- This action is only available to Brivo Account Config Tool Administrators
- Assistant Administrators must have view and edit permissions to a site to change the schedule state of the associated access point

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/schedules/change-state/{accessPointId}
```

## Header

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Accept-version | version | The version of the endpoint which will receive the request. The header is required in order to call what we now consider to be the default implementation of this endpoint. |

- [Header-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#header-examples-Access_Point-Door_Override-0_0_0-0)

```json
"Accept-version" : "2.0"
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| accessPointId | Number | The id associated with the access point |

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| endTimeMode | Text | Determines how the override will end. Possible values are:<br>- `UNTIL_TIME`<br>  - The override will stay in effect until a specified time.<br>- `UNTIL_NEXT_SCHEDULE_CHANGE`<br>  - The override will stay in effect until the next time the access point's associated unlock schedule change occurs.<br>  - This mode may only be used for access points which are configured with an unlock schedule.<br>- `INDEFINITE`<br>  - The override will stay in effect until it is manually removed. |
| behavior | Text | Determines whether the access point should lock, or unlock, while the override is in effect. Possible values are `LOCK` and `UNLOCK` |
| endTime optional | DateTime | Specifies what time the override should end. Supported only when `endTimeMode` is `UNTIL_TIME`. |

- [UntilTime-Example](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Access_Point-Door_Override-0_0_0-0)
- [UntilNextScheduleChange-Example](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Access_Point-Door_Override-0_0_0-1)
- [Indefinite-Example](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Access_Point-Door_Override-0_0_0-2)

```json
{
    "endTimeMode": "UNTIL_TIME",
    "behavior": "LOCK",
    "endTime": "2021-01-02T22:00:00Z"
}
```

```json
{
    "endTimeMode": "UNTIL_NEXT_SCHEDULE_CHANGE",
    "behavior": "UNLOCK"
}
```

```json
{
    "endTimeMode": "INDEFINITE",
    "behavior": "LOCK"
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| accessPointName | Text | The name of this access point |
| accessPointState | Text |  |
| accessPointScheduledState | Text | The current base lock/unlock state of the access point, taking into account any schedule, schedule override, and threat level applied; as of the time specified in the `statusUpdated` field. The door input status is NOT reflected in this value, but is reflected in the `accessPointInputState` Value may be `LOCK` or `UNLOCK`, or `UNKNOWN` in the event that the access point's state could not be retrieved or has not yet been set. |
| accessPointInputState | Text | The actual status of the access point according to the door input relay, which takes into account whether the door has been unlocked (e.g. via an admin pulse or presenting a credential) in addition to the scheduled unlock state. |
| statusUpdated optional | DateTime | The timestamp for when the `accessPointState` was retrieved. This field is not included if the state is unknown. |
| siteName | Text | The name of the access point's site |
| siteTimezone | Text | The name of the time zone for this access point's site |
| panelName | Text | The name of this access point's control panel |
| panelCpNumber | Text | The CP number of this access point's control panel |
| canPanelSupportScheduleOverride | Boolean | Whether or not this control panel can support door override. Door Override is supported by ACS100, ACS300, ACS6000 and ACS-SDC panels with firmware version 6.1.4 or higher. |
| unlockSchedule optional | UnlockSchedule | Describes the access point's unlock schedule, if one is configured. |
| scheduleOverride optional | DoorOverride | Describes the access point's current door override, if one is in effect. |

## UnlockSchedule

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The ID of the unlock schedule |
| name | Text | The name of the unlock schedule |
| isScheduleBlockActive | Boolean | Whether this unlock schedule is currently active. If the access point is scheduled to be unlocked, this will be `true`. |
| nextTimeChange | DateTime | The next time that this unlock schedule will change state. |

## DoorOverride

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| endTimeMode | Text | The end time mode of the override. Possible values are:<br>- `UNTIL_TIME`<br>  - The override will stay in effect until a specified time.<br>- `UNTIL_NEXT_SCHEDULE_CHANGE`<br>  - The override will stay in effect until the next time the access point's associated unlock schedule change occurs.<br>- `INDEFINITE`<br>  - The override will stay in effect until it is manually removed. |
| behavior | Text | Whether the override is to lock or unlock the access point. Possible values are `LOCK` and `UNLOCK`. |
| endTime optional | DateTime | The time at which the override will end. Not present when `endTimeMode` is `INDEFINITE`. |

- [Success-Response](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Access_Point-Door_Override-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "accessPointName": "Front Door",
    "accessPointState": "UNLOCKED",
    "statusUpdated": "2020-04-17T18:23:52Z"
    "siteName": "HQ Site",
    "siteTimezone": "US/Eastern",
    "panelName": "Panel THB-XJ-YYBIR",
    "panelCpNumber": "THB-XJ-YYBIR",
    "canPanelSupportScheduleOverride": true,
    "unlockSchedule": {
        "id": 1111,
        "name": "9-5 Monday-Friday",
        "isScheduleBlockActive": true,
        "nextTimeChange": "2020-04-17T21:00:00Z"
    },
    "scheduleOverride": {
        "endTimeMode": "UNTIL_TIME",
        "behavior": "UNLOCK",
        "endTime": "2020-04-18T00:00:00Z"
    }
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided door override is invalid or contains field values invalid for the specified access point |
| 403 | Forbidden, you do not have permission to change the schedule state of this access point |
| 404 | Not Found, the access point specified does not exist or is not accessible |
| 412 | Precondition failed, the access point does not support overrides or one is already in effect |
| 417 | Expectation failed, setting the override failed due to an offline control panel or network communication error |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-Door_Override-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-Door_Override-0_0_0-1)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-Door_Override-0_0_0-2)
- [412 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-Door_Override-0_0_0-3)
- [417 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-Door_Override-0_0_0-4)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
    "code": 400,
    "message": "Cannot use mode UNTIL_NEXT_SCHEDULE_CHANGE; This door does not have an unlock schedule."
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
    "code": 403,
    "message": "Access to the requested resource was denied"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
    "code": 404,
    "message": "Unknown Access Point"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 412 Precondition Failed
{
    "code": 412,
    "message": "This door already has a schedule override"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 417 Expectation Failed
{
    "code": 417,
    "message": "Could not reach device to send it your schedule override."
}
```

# Access\_Point - Elevator Activation

Unlocks an Elevator the Administrators request.

- Administrator must have permission to unlock the elevator

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/access-points/{accessPointId}/activateElevator
```

- [Filter-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#examples-Access_Point-ActivateElevator-0_0_0-0)

```text
/access-points/12345/activateElevator
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| accessPointId | number | The id associated with the accesspoint |

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| pulseTime | Long | Floor pulse duration in seconds (between 1 - 600) |

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| targetDevices | Long\[\] | the OID of floor devices |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Access_Point-ActivateElevator-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "pulseTime"  : 1,
  "targetDevices": [1,2,3]
}
```

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Access_Point-ActivateElevator-0_0_0-0)

```text
HTTP/1.1 200 Success
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 404 | Not Found, the access point specified does not exist or is not accessible |
| 412 | Precondition failed, the specified access point is not connected |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-ActivateElevator-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-ActivateElevator-0_0_0-1)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-ActivateElevator-0_0_0-2)

```json
{

  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```


# Access\_Point - Live Status

Retrieve live status information for an access point

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/device-status/{accessPointId}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| accessPointName | Text | The name of this access point |
| accessPointState | Text |  |
| accessPointScheduledState | Text | The current base lock/unlock state of the access point, taking into account any schedule, schedule override, and threat level applied; as of the time specified in the `statusUpdated` field. The door input status is NOT reflected in this value, but is reflected in the `accessPointInputState` Value may be `LOCK` or `UNLOCK`, or `UNKNOWN` in the event that the access point's state could not be retrieved or has not yet been set. |
| accessPointInputState | Text | The actual status of the access point according to the door input relay, which takes into account whether the door has been unlocked (e.g. via an admin pulse or presenting a credential) in addition to the scheduled unlock state. |
| statusUpdated optional | DateTime | The timestamp for when the `accessPointState` was retrieved. This field is not included if the state is unknown. |
| siteName | Text | The name of the access point's site |
| siteTimezone | Text | The name of the time zone for this access point's site |
| panelName | Text | The name of this access point's control panel |
| panelCpNumber | Text | The CP number of this access point's control panel |
| canPanelSupportScheduleOverride | Boolean | Whether or not this control panel can support door override. Door Override is supported by ACS100, ACS300, ACS6000 and ACS-SDC panels with firmware version 6.1.4 or higher. |
| unlockSchedule optional | UnlockSchedule | Describes the access point's unlock schedule, if one is configured. |
| scheduleOverride optional | DoorOverride | Describes the access point's current door override, if one is in effect. |

## UnlockSchedule

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The ID of the unlock schedule |
| name | Text | The name of the unlock schedule |
| isScheduleBlockActive | Boolean | Whether this unlock schedule is currently active. If the access point is scheduled to be unlocked, this will be `true`. |
| nextTimeChange | DateTime | The next time that this unlock schedule will change state. |

## DoorOverride

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| endTimeMode | Text | The end time mode of the override. Possible values are:<br>- `UNTIL_TIME`<br>  - The override will stay in effect until a specified time.<br>- `UNTIL_NEXT_SCHEDULE_CHANGE`<br>  - The override will stay in effect until the next time the access point's associated unlock schedule change occurs.<br>- `INDEFINITE`<br>  - The override will stay in effect until it is manually removed. |
| behavior | Text | Whether the override is to lock or unlock the access point. Possible values are `LOCK` and `UNLOCK`. |
| endTime optional | DateTime | The time at which the override will end. Not present when `endTimeMode` is `INDEFINITE`. |

- [Success-Response](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Access_Point-Live_Status-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "accessPointName": "Front Door",
    "accessPointState": "UNLOCKED",
    "statusUpdated": "2020-04-17T18:23:52Z"
    "siteName": "HQ Site",
    "siteTimezone": "US/Eastern",
    "panelName": "Panel THB-XJ-YYBIR",
    "panelCpNumber": "THB-XJ-YYBIR",
    "canPanelSupportScheduleOverride": true,
    "unlockSchedule": {
        "id": 1111,
        "name": "9-5 Monday-Friday",
        "isScheduleBlockActive": true,
        "nextTimeChange": "2020-04-17T21:00:00Z"
    },
    "scheduleOverride": {
        "endTimeMode": "UNTIL_TIME",
        "behavior": "UNLOCK",
        "endTime": "2020-04-18T00:00:00Z"
    }
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 404 | Not Found, the access point specified does not exist or is not accessible |

- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Access_Point-Live_Status-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
    "code": 404,
    "message": "Unknown Access Point"
}
```

# Access\_Point - Unlock Access Point

Sends a request to unlock an access-point.

- The request will be granted if the card holder has permission to access this door based on their groups affiliation.
- Available only to digital credential users

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/access-points/{accessPointId}/unlock
```

## RequestBody

# Account - Account Listing

Retrieve a listing of accounts.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/accounts
```

- [Filter-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#examples-Account-AccountsList-0_0_0-0)

```text
/accounts?filter=name__eq:Acme+Inc
```

## ?QueryParam

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | number | The offset of values before returning the first result.<br>Default value: `0` |
| pageSize optional | number | The number of records to return in a Page.<br>Default value: `20`<br>Size range: `1-100` |

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| filter optional | text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are<br>- `name`<br>  - Filters based on an account's name<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any account with a name that contains the provided name value |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | Account\[\] | Listing of Account Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |
| count | Number | Total count of results available for criteria |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Account-AccountsList-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "data": [\
    {\
      "id": 304608,\

      "accountType" : "ONAIR",\
      "masterAdmin": {\
          "username": "testing01",\
          "firstName": "Road",\
          "lastName": "Runner"\
      }\
    },\

      "id": 304796,\
      "name": "AB",\

      "accountType" : "ONAIR",\
```

# Account - List Account Settings

Provides a listing of the viewable settings associated with the account

```html

```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| accountOid | Number | The object Id of the account. |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | AccountSetting\[\] | The listing of account settings |
| count | Number | The name associated with the account |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Account-AccountSettingsList-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
 "data" : [{\
              "id"          : 4312,\
              "name"        : "ACCOUNT_SETTING_OPTION",\
              "value"       : "CURRENT_VALUE",\
              "defaultValue": "DEFAULT_VALUE"\
            },\
            {\
              "id"          : 2715,\
              "name"        : "MAX_ALLOWED",\
              "value"       : "10",\
              "defaultValue": "10"\
            }],
 "count": 2
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 404 | Not Found, the specified account was not found |

- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Account-AccountSettingsList-0_0_0-0)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Account-AccountSettingsList-0_0_0-1)

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "Account not found"
}
```

# Account - Update Account Setting

Update an account setting. The following account settings cannot be updated from API and the endpoint will return a 403 Forbidden error, as they can only be updated from Partner Portal:

- MOBILE\_PASS\_ALLOTMENT (settingId = 1)
- NFC\_CREDENTIAL\_ENABLED (settingId = 12)
- BLOCK\_ONAIR (settingId = 13)
- SUPPRESS\_EVENTS (settingId = 14)
- NFC\_ALLOTMENT (settingId = 19)
- BRIVO\_ALLEGION\_MOBILE\_PASS (settingId = 26)
- BRIVO\_ALLEGION\_MOBILE\_PASS\_ALLOTMENT (settingId = 27)

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/accounts/{accountOid}/settings/{settingId}
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| accountOid | Number | The object Id of the account. |
| settingId | Number | The Id of the account setting to be updated. |

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| value | Text | The value to update the specified setting to. |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Account-AccountSettingsUpdate-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "value" : "42"
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id of the account setting |
| name | Text | The name associated with the account setting |
| value | Text | The current value being applied to the account setting |
| defaultValue | Text | The default value assigned when no specific value is set |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Account-AccountSettingsUpdate-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "id"          : 2715,
  "name"        : "MAX_ALLOWED",
  "value"       : "42",
  "defaultValue": "10"
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 404 | Not Found, the specified account was not found |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Account-AccountSettingsUpdate-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Account-AccountSettingsUpdate-0_0_0-1)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Account-AccountSettingsUpdate-0_0_0-2)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "Account not found"
}
```

# Account - Update Account

Updates an existing account that is associated with the account Id given.

- This action is only available to Brivo Account Config Tool Dealers who own the account and CSRs.

- If the account being updated is a dealer account you need the billing and emergency contact.

  - The address is not necessary for the emergency contact.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/accounts/{accountId}
```

## RequestBody

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| name | Text | Name of the account |
| description optional | Text | Description of the account |
| contact | Contact | The main contact information for the account |
| emergency | Contact | The emergency contact information for the account (Dealer account only) |
| billing | Contact | The billing contact information for the account (Dealer account only) |

## RequestBody, contact:

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| firstName | Text | The first name of the main contact for the account |
| lastName | Text | The last name of the main contact for the account |
| streetAddress1 | Text | The street address for the account account contact, line 1 |
| streetAddress2 optional | Text | The street address for the account account contact, line 2 |
| city | Text | The city for the account account contact |
| state | Text | The state or province of the account contact |
| country optional | Text | The country of the account contact |
| postalCode | Text | The postal code of the account contact |
| telephoneNumber | Text | The account contact's phone number |
| telephoneExtension optional | Text | The account contact's phone extension |
| email optional | Text | The account contact email |
| notes optional | Text | The account contact's notes (this can only be updated on a contact by a CSR) |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Account-UpdateAccount-0_0_0-0)

```json
 {
     "name" : "Acme Corp",
     "description" : "Acme Operation North Division",
     "contact" :
	{
		"streetAddress1" : "413 Cheshire Way",
		"city" : "ThisWay",
		"state" : "Underland",
		"postalCode" : "21255",
		"country" : "United States",
		"telephoneNumber" : "222-333-1111",
		"telephoneExtension" : "33",
		"firstName" : "Alice",
		"lastName" : "Carroll"
	}
}
```

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Account-UpdateAccount-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
        "id": "485386",
        "name" : "Acme Corp",
        "description" : "Acme Operation North Division",
        "accountNumber" : "2725390726",
        "accountType" : "ONAIR",
        "contact" :
	        {
            "streetAddress1" : "413 Cheshire Way",
            "city" : "ThisWay",
            "state" : "Underland",
            "postalCode" : "21255",
            "country" : "United States",
            "telephoneNumber" : "222-333-1111",
            "telephoneExtension" : "33",
            "firstName" : "Alice",
            "lastName" : "Carroll"
	      },
        "masterAdmin" :
        {
            "username" : "QueenOfHearts",
            "firstName" : "Elsie",
            "lastName" : "Lacie",
            "email" : "elacie@acme.com"
        }
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 404 | Not Found, the specified account was not found |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Account-UpdateAccount-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Account-UpdateAccount-0_0_0-1)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Account-UpdateAccount-0_0_0-2)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

```json
{
  "code"    : 403,

}
```

```json
{

  "message" : "Account not found"
```

# Activity

# Activity - Activity Listing

\*\*DEPRECATED - The [/events](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#api-Event-ListEvent) listing endpoint will now be the actively developed event listing \*\*

Retrieve a listing of activity events

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/activities
```

- [Filter-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#examples-Activity-ListActivity-0_0_0-0)

```text
/activities?filter=access-point__eq:111111
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | number | Listed results will display beginning from the offset value. |
| pageSize optional | number | The maximum number of records that will be returned for the call starting from the offset value.<br>Size range: `1-100` |
| filter optional | text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are<br>- `site`<br>  <br>  - Filter based on the site id that an activity is associated with.<br>  - Multiple id values can be passed by comma separating them.<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any activity from the site ids provided<br>- `user`<br>  <br>  - Filter based on the entity id who is responsible for the activity<br>  - Multiple id values can be passed by comma separating them.<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any activity from the user ids provided<br>- `object`<br>  <br>  - Filter based on the object id that the activity is referencing<br>  - Multiple id values can be passed by comma separating them<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any activity from the object ids provided<br>- `device`<br>  <br>  - Filter based on the device id that the activity is referencing<br>  - Multiple id values can be passed by comma separating them<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any activity from the device ids provided<br>- `camera`<br>  <br>  - Filter based on the camera id that the activity is referencing<br>  - Multiple id values can be passed by comma separating them<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any activity from the camera ids provided<br>- `access-point`<br>  <br>  - Filter based on the access-point id that the activity is referencing<br>  - Multiple id values can be passed by comma separating them<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any activity from the access-point ids provided<br>- `event_type`<br>  <br>  - Filter based on the types of events specified by the provided event-types<br>  - Multiple event-types can be provided by comma separation<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes activities from the provided event-types<br>  - Valid event types<br>    - `camera` \- events related to camera activities<br>    - `exception` \- events that occur outside of normal operation such as unknown credentials<br>    - `non_exception` \- normal, expected events such as successful access events<br>- `occurred`<br>  <br>  - Filter based on the activity occurred time<br>  - A maximum occurred window of 24 hours is enforced<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Searches for activity events on the day specified, disregarding the time values<br>    - gt: Searches for events after a specified date and time value<br>    - lt: Searches for events before a specified date and time value<br>  - Providing both an `occurred__gt` and `occurred__lt` will allow specifying a specific date range<br>  - Providing only an `occurred__gt` filter will search for the 24 hours after the provided date<br>  - Providing only an `occurred__lt` filter will search for the 24 hours prior to the provided date |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | Activity\[\] | Listing of Activity Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |
| count | Number | Total count of results available for criteria |

- [Success-Response](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Activity-ListActivity-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
 "offset"  : 0,
 "pageSize": 20,
 "count"   : 2,
 "data"    : [{\
               "id"           : 11111111,\
               "occurred"     : "2015-05-01T14:35:50Z",\
               "siteId"       : 9999,\
               "siteName"     : "Site 1",\
               "userId"       : 333333,\
               "objectId"     : 444444,\
               "objectType"   : "ACCESS-POINT",\
               "objectName"   : "Front door",\
               "actionTypeId" : 5018,\
               "description"  : "Failed Access by John Smith: Unauthorized Access Attempt"\
               },\
               {\
               "id"           : 11112222,\
               "occurred"     : "2015-04-30T20:07:59Z",\
               "siteId"       : 9999,\
               "siteName"     : "Site 1",\
               "userId"       : 555555,\
               "objectId"     : 777777,\
               "objectType"   : "ACCESS-POINT",\
               "objectName"   : "Side door",\
               "actionTypeId" : 2004,\
               "description"  : "User Entry"\
             }]
 }
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, Invalid criteria were provided for the listing call |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Activity-ListActivity-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
 "code"    : 400,
 "message" : "Invalid listing criteria provided"
}
```

# Administrator - Administrator Listing

Retrieve a listing of administrators.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/administrators
```

- [Filter-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#examples-Administrator-AdminList-0_0_0-0)

```text
/administrators?filter=username__eq:john.deo
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | number | The offset of values before returning the first result.<br>Default value: `0` |
| pageSize optional | number | The number of records to return in a Page.<br>Default value: `20`<br>Size range: `1-100` |
| filter optional | text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are<br>- `username`<br>  <br>  - Filters based on a administrator's username<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any administrators with a username that contains the provided name value<br>- `type`<br>  <br>  - Filter based on the type of administrators specified by the provided type<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes administrators from the provided type<br>    - Valid type<br>      - `csr` \- csr administrators<br>      - `dealer` \- dealer administrators<br>      - `master` \- master administrators<br>      - `senior` \- senior administrators<br>      - `assistant` \- assistant administrators |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | Administrator\[\] | Listing of Administrator Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |
| count | Number | Total count of results available for criteria |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Administrator-AdminList-0_0_0-0)

```json
 {
    "data": [\
      {\
        "id": 314761,\
        "username": "minasmythe",\
        "firstName": "Mina",\
        "lastName": "Smythe",\
        "identityType": "ASSISTANT",\
        "email": "mina.smythet@brivo.com",\
        "timezone": "US/Eastern",\
        "canCreateAdmins": false\
      },\
      {\
        "id": 314815,\
        "username": "johndoe",\
        "firstName": "John",\
        "lastName": "Doe",\
        "identityType": "ASSISTANT",\
        "email": "john.doe@brivo.com",\
        "timezone": "US/Central",\
        "canCreateAdmins": false\
      }\
    ],
    "offset": 2,
    "pageSize": 2,
    "count": 42
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, Invalid criteria were provided for the listing call |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Administrator-AdminList-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
 "code"    : 400,
 "message" : "Invalid listing criteria provided"
}
```

# Administrator - Create Administrator

Create a new administrator

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/administrators
```

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| username | Text | Administrator's username |
| firstName | Text | First name |
| middleName optional | Text | Middle name |
| lastName | Text | Last name |
| email | Text | The contact e-mail address for the administrator.<br>This e-mail will be used for password recovery.<br>The e-mail address is considered invalid if it contains one of these characters: , : ; < > ( ) \[ \] \ / " ' ~ ! # $ % ^ & \* = { } \| ? \` (whitespace) |
| securityQuestion | Text | The challenge question used during password recovery. |
| identityType optional | Text | The type of identityType you wish to create. Allowed values: `ASSISTANT, SENIOR, DEALER` |
| canCreateAdmins optional | boolean | Dictates whether admin, you are about to create, has the ability to create admins or not. This attribute can `ONLY` be specified when creating `identityType: SENIOR`. |
| securityAnswer | Text | Answer to the securityQuestion provided |
| timezone optional | Text | The time zone to associate with the administrator.<br>If `timezone` is not provided, it will default to the timezone associated with the primary account administrator. |
| password optional | Text | If `password` is not provided, a temporary password will be emailed to the administrator |

- [Request-Body:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Administrator-AdminCreate-0_0_0-0)
- [Request-Body:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Administrator-AdminCreate-0_0_0-1)
- [Request-Body:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Administrator-AdminCreate-0_0_0-2)

```json

{
    "username"         : "acme1357",
    "firstName"        : "James",
    "middleName"       : "Robert",
    "lastName"         : "Miller",
    "email"            : "james.miller@acme.com",
    "securityQuestion" : "First pet's name",
    "securityAnswer"   : "Rex",
    "identityType"     : "SENIOR",
    "canCreateAdmins"  : false,
    "timezone"         : "US/Eastern",
    "password"         : "BrivoIstheB3st"
}
```

```json

{
    "username"         : "acme1357",
    "firstName"        : "James",
    "middleName"       : "Robert",
    "lastName"         : "Miller",
    "email"            : "james.miller@acme.com",
    "securityQuestion" : "First pet's name",
    "securityAnswer"   : "Rex",
    "identityType"     : "SENIOR",
    "canCreateAdmins"  : true,
    "timezone"         : "US/Eastern",
    "password"         : "BrivoIstheB3st"
}
```

```json

{
    "username"         : "acme1357",
    "firstName"        : "James",
    "middleName"       : "Robert",
    "lastName"         : "Miller",
    "email"            : "james.miller@acme.com",
    "securityQuestion" : "First pet's name",
    "securityAnswer"   : "Rex",
    "identityType"     : "SENIOR",
    "canCreateAdmins"  : true,
    "timezone"         : "US/Eastern",
    "password"         : "BrivoIstheB3st"
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id associated with the administrator |
| username | Text | Administrator's username |
| firstName | Text | First name |
| middleName | Text | Middle name |
| lastName | Text | Last name |
| email | Text | Contact email address |
| timezone | Text | Administrator's Time zone |
| identityType | Text | identityType |
| canCreateAdmins | boolean | Does the admin have an ability to create other admins? |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Administrator-AdminCreate-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 200 Success
{
    "id"         : 9876543210,
    "username"   : "acme1357",
    "firstName"  : "James",
    "middleName" : "Robert",
    "lastName"   : "Miller",
    "identityType": "SENIOR",
    "email"      : "james.miller@acme.com",
    "timezone"   : "US/Eastern",
    "canCreateAdmins": false
}
```

# Administrator - Update Administrator

Update the administrator associated with the provided id value

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/administrators/{administratorId}
```

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| firstName | Text | First name |
| middleName optional | Text | Middle name |
| lastName | Text | Last name |
| email | Text | The contact e-mail address for the administrator.<br>This e-mail will be used for password recovery. <br>The e-mail address is considered invalid if it contains one of these characters: , : ; < > ( ) \[ \] \ / " ' ~ ! # $ % ^ & \* = { } \| ? \` (whitespace) |
| identityType optional | Text | The type of identityType you wish to update. <br>Example of legal values: `ASSISTANT, SENIOR, DEALER`. <br>Note: <br>- `IdentityType` is `required` when `canCreateAdmins is true` |
| canCreateAdmins optional | boolean | canCreateAdmins <br>Note: <br>- `canCreateAdmins` is `required` when `IdentityType is SENIOR` |
| timezone optional | Text | The time zone to associate with the administrator.<br>If `timezone` is not provided, it will be the timezone associated with the administrator. |

- [Request-Body:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Administrator-AdminUpdate-0_0_0-0)

```json

{
    "id"               : 314761,
    "username"         : "acme1357",
    "firstName"        : "James",
    "middleName"       : "Robert",
    "lastName"         : "Miller",
    "email"            : "james.miller@acme.com",
    "identityType"     : "SENIOR",
    "canCreateAdmins"  : false,
    "timezone"         : "US/Eastern",
    "accountId"        : 123445
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id associated with the administrator |
| username | Text | Administrator's username |
| firstName | Text | First name |
| middleName | Text | Middle name |
| lastName | Text | Last name |
| email | Text | Contact email address |
| timezone | Text | Administrator's Time zone |
| identityType | Text | identityType |
| canCreateAdmins | boolean | Does the admin have an ability to create other admins? |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Administrator-AdminUpdate-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 200 Success
{
    "id"         : 9876543210,
    "username"   : "acme1357",
    "firstName"  : "James",
    "middleName" : "Robert",
    "lastName"   : "Miller",
    "identityType": "SENIOR",
    "email"      : "james.miller@acme.com",
    "timezone"   : "US/Eastern",
    "canCreateAdmins": false
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, Invalid Admin criteria |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |

# Administrator - Update Login

Updates the login status associated with the Administrator

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/administrators/{administratorId}/login
```

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| active optional | Text | Sets the login's active status |
| password optional | Text | The password to set.<br>Required if `temporaryPassword` is provided. |
| temporaryPassword optional | Boolean | Sets the password's as temporary status.<br>If `temporaryPassword` is not provided, the new `password` will not be saved as temporary. |
| securityQuestion optional | Text | The challenge question used during password recovery.<br>Required if `securityAnswer` is provided. |
| securityAnswer optional | Text | Answer to the securityQuestion provided.<br>Required if `securityQuestion` is provided. |
| expiration optional | DateTime | The expiration date of the login. |

- [Request-Body:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Administrator-UpdateLogin-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "active"           : "true",
    "password"         : "BrivoIsTheB3st",
    "temporaryPassword": "true",
    "securityQuestion" : "What is your favorite color?",
    "securityAnswer"   : "Maroon",
    "expiration"       : "2022-10-16T22:14:128Z"
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| active | Boolean | The active state of the login |
| locked | Boolean | The lock state of the login |
| temporaryPassword | Boolean | If true, the passsword is temporary |
| securityQuestion | Text | Password Reset Security Question |
| retryCount | Integer | Counter for failed login attempts. |
| lastAttempted | DateTime | DateTime of the last login attempt. |
| temporaryPasswordExpiration | DateTime | Expiration date of the temporary password. |
| expiration | DateTime | Expiration date of the login. |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Administrator-UpdateLogin-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 200 Success
{
    "active"                     : true,
    "locked"                     : false,
    "temporaryPassword"          : true,
    "securityQuestion"           : "What is your favorite color?",
    "retryCount"                 : 3,
    "lastAttempted"              : "2016-10-16T18:14:128Z",
    "temporaryPasswordExpiration": "2016-10-16T22:14:128Z",
```

# Application - Create New Application

Create a new Application.

- In order to create an application that uses the 3-Legged work flow the "authorization\_code" and "refresh\_token" Grant Types should be specified. If "authorization\_code" is specified as a Grant Type then the password grant cannot also be specified and a redirect URI must be specified correctly.
- If the "password" grant type is specified then the Application can only be used to access the owning Account and no other. Also if the "password" Grant Type is specified then the "authorization\_code" Grant Type cannot be specified and the redirect URI field can be omitted.
- The Access Tokens are short lived as we are using JWT tokens which carry the Authentication, Application information, User Principal, and expiration.
- If you wish to use our tokens as a valid authentication for your integration the the Tokens can be validated by checking the signature using the certificate end point: GET https://auth.brivo.com/oauth/token\_key.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/applications
```

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| name | Text | The application name |
| description | Text | Description of the application |
| redirectUri optional | Text | The redirect URI for the application. |
| grantTypes | GrantType | The array of grant types for this application |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Application-ApplicationCreate-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
     "name"    : "Mobile One Administrative Application",
     "description"   : "3rd Party Administrative mobile application",
     "redirectUri"     : "mobileone://mobile.deeplink/approval_receieved",
     "grantTypes"   : ["authorization_code","refresh_token"]
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The ID assigned to the application. |
| accountId | Number | The Account Id of the account which created the application. |
| name | Text | The Name of the application. |
| description | Text | The application's description. |
| grantTypes | Text | Methods used to request authorization |
| clientId | Text | The application's Client ID. |
| secret | Text | The application's client Secret. |
| accessTokenTtl | Number | Access token time |
| refreshTokenTtl | Number | Refresh token time |
| created | DateTime | The time the application was created. |
| updated | DateTime | The last update time of the application. |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Application-ApplicationCreate-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "id" : 2452345,
    "accountId":502252,
    "name" : "clientApplicationName",
    "description" : "the clientAppDescription",
    "grantTypes" : ["password","refresh_token","authorization_code"],
    "clientId" : "4cd67df7-7b96-46ab-b289-b74ff11374a3",
    "secret": "fv2pB8EWTm2QhLDwy0zAy3WfqT6xoSQl",
    "accessTokenTtl": 60,
    "refreshTokenTtl": 1209600,
    "created":"2015-08-01T21:33:34Z",
    "updated":"2015-08-01T21:33:34Z"
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Application-ApplicationCreate-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Application-ApplicationCreate-0_0_0-1)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```
