# Assignments

# Assignments - Configure admin assignments

Configure admin assignments. Limit the administrator to manage users in the selected user groups, devices in the selected sites, and emergency scenarios. You can allow or disallow all via the assignmentType parameter ("ALL" or "NONE" respectively), or specify specific entries by using an assignmentType value of "SELECTED", and listing the individual entries via the "selectedIds" parameter.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/assignments/{administratorId}
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| administratorId | number | The ID of the administrator for which the assignments are configured |

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| sites | Assignment | The assignments that the administrator has to the sites<br>- `assignmentType` The type of assignment to the sites. Can be "ALL", "NONE", or "SELECTED"<br>- `selectedIds` The list of site IDs that the administrator has assignments to. This field is to be used when the assignmentType is "SELECTED" |
| groups | Assignment | The assignments that the administrator has to the groups<br>- `assignmentType` The type of assignment to the groups. Can be "ALL", "NONE", or "SELECTED"<br>- `selectedIds` The list of group IDs that the administrator has assignments to. This field is to be used when the assignmentType is "SELECTED" |
| emergencyScenarios | Assignment | The assignments that the administrator has to the emergency scenarios<br>- `assignmentType` The type of assignment to the emergency scenarios. Can be "ALL", "NONE", or "SELECTED"<br>- `selectedIds` The list of emergency scenario IDs that the administrator has assignments to. This field is to be used when the assignmentType is "SELECTED" |

- [Request-Body:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Assignments-replaceAdminAssignments-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "sites":{
        "assignmentType":"ALL"
    },
    "groups":{
        "assignmentType":"SELECTED",
        "selectedIds":[111,222]
    },
    "emergencyScenarios":{
        "assignmentType":"NONE"
    }
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| sites | AssignmentSelection | The assignments that the administrator has to the sites<br>- `isAll` Field which specifies if the administrator has assignments to all the site entries. If the field is true, the assignments array field will be empty. If it is false, the assignments array will be either empty, meaning that the administrator has no assignments (none), or will have the list of the individual selected assignments<br>- `assignments` The listing of Site objects that the administratorId has assignments to<br>- `name` The name of the site<br>- `id` The id of the site |
| groups | AssignmentSelection | The assignments that the administrator has on the groups<br>- `isAll` Field which specifies if the administrator has assignments to all the groups entries. If the field is true, the assignments array field will be empty. If it is false, the assignments array will be either empty, meaning that the administrator has no assignments (none), or will have the list of the individual selected assignments<br>- `assignments` The listing of Groups objects that the administratorId has assignments to<br>- `name` The name of the group<br>- `id` The id of the group |
| emergencyScenario | AssignmentSelection | The assignments that the administrator has to the emergency scenario<br>- `isAll` Field which specifies if the administrator has assignments to all the emergency scenario entries. If the field is true, the assignments array field will be empty. If it is false, the assignments array will be either empty, meaning that the administrator has no assignments (none), or will have the list of the individual selected assignments<br>- `assignments` The listing of Emergency Scenario objects that the administratorId has assignments to<br>- `name` The name of the emergency scenario<br>- `id` The id of the emergency scenario |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Assignments-replaceAdminAssignments-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 200 OK
{
  "sites":
    {
      "isAll": true,
      "assignments": []
    },
  "groups":
    {
      "isAll": false,
      "assignments": [\
        {\
          "name": "Group 1",\
          "id": 111\
        },\
        {\
          "name": "Group 2",\
          "id": 222\
        }\
      ]
    },
  "emergencyScenarios":
    {
      "isAll": false,
      "assignments": []
    }
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 404 | Not Found, the specified user was not found |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |

- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Assignments-replaceAdminAssignments-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Assignments-replaceAdminAssignments-0_0_0-1)

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "Administrator with id administratorId does not exist"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

# Camera - Camera Listing

Retrieve a listing of cameras.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/cameras
```

- [Filter-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#examples-Camera-CamerasList-0_0_0-0)

```text
/cameras?filter=name__eq:Front+Door+Camera
```

## ?QueryParam

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | number | The offset of values before returning the first result.<br>Default value: `0` |
| pageSize optional | number | The number of records to return in a Page.<br>Default value: `20`<br>Size range: `1-100` |

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| filter optional | text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are<br>- `name`<br>  - Filters based on a camera's name<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any camera with a name that contains the provided name value |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | Camera\[\] | Listing of Camera Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |
| count | Number | Total count of results available for criteria |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Camera-CamerasList-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "data": [\
    {\
      "id": 8675309,\
       "name": "Back Door Camera",\
       "videoProvider" : {\
          "type" : "EAGLE_EYE"\
        },\
        "site": {\
          "id" : 789342,\
          "siteName": "Acme West Site"\
        }\
    },\
    {\
      "id": 8675319,\
       "name": "Side Door Camera",\
       "videoProvider" : {\
          "type" : "EAGLE_EYE_CAMERA_MANAGER"\
        },\
        "site": {\
          "id" : 789342,\
          "siteName": "Acme West Site"\
        }\
    },     *\
    {\
      "id": 903768,\
      "name": "Front Door Camera",\
      "videoProvider"     : {\
          "type" : "ONAIR",\
          "version" : "2.22"\
      },\
      "site" : {\
          "id" : 789342,\
          "siteName": "Acme West Site"\
      }\
    }\
  ],
  "offset": 0,
  "pageSize": 20,
  "count": 2
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, Invalid listing criteria specified |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Camera-CamerasList-0_0_0-0)

```json

{
   "code"    : 400,
   "message" : "Invalid listing criteria provided"
}
```

# Camera - Camera Retrieval

Retrieve a camera based on its id

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/cameras/{cameraId}
```

- [Filter-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#examples-Camera-RetrieveCamera-0_0_0-0)

```text
/cameras/12345?showStatus=true
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| cameraId | Number | The id for camera to find |

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| showStatus optional | Boolean | Request camera status with the camera retrieval.<br>Default value: `false` |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id associated with the camera |
| name | Text | The camera's name |
| liveViewUrl | Text | The live view url of the camera |
| site | Site | The site associated with the camera |
| id | Number | The id of the site |
| siteName | Text | The site name |
| status | Text | The camera's current status (only shows when showStatus is set to true) |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Camera-RetrieveCamera-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "id"                : 9486127,
  "name"              : "Front door camera",
  "liveViewUrl"       : "https://acme.cameras.com/1",
  "videoProvider"     : {
     "type" : "EAGLE_EYE"
  },
  "site"              : {
     "id":  321,
     "siteName": "Acme West Site"
  }
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 404 | Not Found, the specified camera was not found |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |

- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Camera-RetrieveCamera-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Camera-RetrieveCamera-0_0_0-1)

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "Camera not found"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

# Camera - Camera Video Clip Listing

Retrieve a listing of camera video clips.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/cameras/{cameraId}/video
```

- [Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#examples-Camera-CameraVideoClipList-0_0_0-0)

```text
/cameras/{cameraId}/video?startTime=2024-05-29T16:00:00Z&endTime=2024-05-29T16:01:00Z
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| startTime | DateTime | Start time to retrieve video clips |
| endTime | DateTime | End time to retrieve video clips |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| startTime | DateTime | The start time of the video clip search |
| endTime | DateTime | The end time of the video clip search |
| cameraObject | CameraObject | The camera object |
| id | Number | The id of the camera |
| name | Text | The name of the camera |
| videoProvider | VideoProviderObject | The video provider object |
| type | Text | The type of video provider |
| siteObject | SiteObject | The site object |
| id | Number | The id of the site |
| name | Text | The name of the site |
| videoClipObject | VideoClipObject\[\] | Listing of Video Clip Objects |
| format | Text | The format of the video clip |
| startTime | DateTime | The start time of the video clip |
| endTime | DateTime | The end time of the video clip. This must be less than 24 hours after startTime. |
| url | Text | The url of the video clip to view or download |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Camera-CameraVideoClipList-0_0_0-0)

```json
     "type" : "EAGLE_EYE"
   },

     "siteName": "Acme Systems"
   }
 },
 "videoClips": [\
   {\
    "format"     : "mp4",\

  },\
   {\
    "format"     : "mp4",\
    "startTime"  : "2016-04-04T09:52:28.512Z",\
    "endTime"    : "2016-04-04T09:52:32.514Z",\
    "url": "https://brivo-videocache.s3.us-east-1.amazonaws.com/....."\
  }\
 ]
}
```

# Control Panel

# Control\_Panel - Get Control Panel Listing

Retrieve a listing of control panels which the current user has view permissions for.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/control-panels
```

- [Filter-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#examples-Control_Panel-ListControlPanels-0_0_0-0)

```text
/control-panels?filter=status__eq:connected
```

## ?QueryParam

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset | Number | The offset of values before returning the first result. |
| pageSize | Number | The number of records to return in a Page. |
| filter optional | Text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>- Available filter criteria are<br>- `status`<br>  - Filters based on a control panel's status<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any control panel that falls under the corresponding status<br>  - Allowed status values<br>    - connected: returns control panels that are connected.<br>    - disconnected: returns control panels that are disconnected. |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | ControlPanel\[\] | Listing of ControlPanel Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |
| count | Number | Total count of results available for criteria |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Control_Panel-ListControlPanels-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
 "offset"  : 0,
 "pageSize": 20,
 "count"   : 2,
 "data"    : [{\
                "id": 271622,\
                "panelName": "cp7946804",\
                "serialNumber": "CP7946804",\
                "activated": "2015-03-25T04:00:00Z",\
                "updated": "2015-07-09T04:00:00Z",\
                "lastContact": "2015-07-13T16:33:55Z",\
                "firmwareVersion": "5.0.19",\
                "panelType": "IRIS V5.0",\
                "status" : "CONNECTED"\
            },\
            {\
                "id": 221314,\
                "panelName": "TestCP",\
                "serialNumber": "CP462088",\
                "activated": "2013-07-10T04:00:00Z",\
                "updated": "2015-07-09T04:00:00Z",\
                "lastContact": "2015-07-13T16:33:55Z",\
                "firmwareVersion": "5.0.20",\
                "panelType": "IRIS V5.0",\
                "status" : "CONNECTED"\
            }]
}
```

## Error code

| --- | --- |

```json
{
    "message": "Invalid criteria provided",
    "code": 400
}
```

# Control\_Panel - Get Control Panel by id

| serialNumber | Text | The serial number associated with the panel |
| activated | DateTime | The date the panel was activated |
| updated | DateTime | The date the panel was last updated |
| firmwareVersion | Text | the software version the panel reports that it has installed |
| status | Text | The control panel's current status |

```json
    "panelName": "cp7946804",
    "serialNumber": "CP7946804",
    "activated": "2015-03-25T04:00:00Z",

    "lastContact": "2015-07-13T16:33:55Z",
    "firmwareVersion": "5.0.19",
```

# Control\_Panel - Get Control Panel firmware

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/control-panels/{controlPanelId}/firmware
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| controlPanelId | Number | the id associated with the Control Panel |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id associated with the panel |
| panelName | Text | The name of the panel |
| serialNumber | Text | The serial number associated with the panel |
| activated | DateTime | The date the panel was activated |
| updated | DateTime | The date the panel was last updated |
| firmwareVersion | Text | the software version the panel reports that it has installed |
| version | Text | The current version of firmware. |
| availableVersions | Text\[\] | The available firmware versions on the panel |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Control_Panel-ControlPanelFirmwareGet-0_0_0-0)

```json

    "firmwareVersion": "5.0.0",
    "availableVersions" : ["5.0.0",\
                           "5.1.0",\
                           "5.1.1b",\
                           "5.2.0",\
                           "5.2.1"]
}
```

# Control\_Panel - Update Control Panel firmware

Update the firmware of a specified Control Panel

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/control-panels/{controlPanelId}/firmware
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| controlPanelId | Number | The id associated with the Control Panel |

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| firmwareVersion | Text | The firmware version to install on the Control Panel |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Control_Panel-ControlPanelFirmwareUpdate-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "firmwareVersion"  : "5.20.0"
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| version | Text | The current version of firmware. |
| availableVersions | Text\[\] | The available firmware versions on the panel |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Control_Panel-ControlPanelFirmwareUpdate-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "firmwareVersion": "5.0.0",
    "availableVersions" : ["5.0.0",\
                           "5.1.0",\
                           "5.1.1b",\
                           "5.2.0",\
                           "5.2.1"]
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided criteria is invalid |
| 404 | Not Found, the provided Control Panel is not found |
| 412 | Precondition Failed, the provided Control Panel is not connected |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Control_Panel-ControlPanelFirmwareUpdate-0_0_0-0)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Control_Panel-ControlPanelFirmwareUpdate-0_0_0-1)
- [412 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Control_Panel-ControlPanelFirmwareUpdate-0_0_0-2)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
    "message": "Invalid criteria provided",
    "code": 400
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
    "message": "Requested control panel not found",
    "code": 404
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 412 Precondition Failed
{
    "message": "Requested control panel is not connected",
    "code": 412
}
```

# Credential

# Credential - Create New Credential

Creates a single credential.

There are two methods which can be used to create a credential:

- Posting the encodedCredential
- Posting the set of field values.

If the encodedCredential is sent that will take precedence over the credential field values. In either case the newly created Credential will be returned with the encodedCredential, the field values, and the credential's ID.

| Supported Credential Formats |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| HID 26 bit | 64-bit BCD PIV | 64-bit Reverse BCD PIV |
| 128-bit PIV | 75-bit PIV | Allegion 34S |
| Casi-Rusco 40 bit | FASC-N | Generic 34 bit (Even) |
| Generic 34 bit (Odd) | HID 33 bit | HID 33 D10202 bit |
| HID 35 bit | HID 37 bit | HID 37 bit w Facility Code |
| HID Corporate 1000 48-bit | PIV-I | Generic 36-bit with Vendor Code |
| 30-bit Wiegand | 32-bit CSN | Allegion 40-Bit |
| AWID 50 bit | HID 36 bit | WaveLynx 56-bit LEAF |
| License plate | EE LPR License plate | Brivo Mobile Credential |
| Brivo Mobile Pass | Unknown format |  |

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/credentials
```

## Parameter

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| credentialFormat | CredentialFormat | The format of the credential to be Created. |
| referenceId | Text | The display or external value of the credential. |
| encodedCredential optional | Text | The hexadecimal representation of the credential.<br>The encodedCredential must include any Parity or Check bits for the credential format. If the exact format of the credential isn't known then use the field values to add the credential.<br>Either the encodedCredential or the fieldValues are required. The encodedCredential will be used if both are specified. |
| size optional | Number | The size in number of bits of the credential to be added. This value needs to match the bit length of the credential format added. If the credentialFormat is of type Unknown format then this size value will be used, otherwise the number of bits for the credential will not be set and will remain NULL. |
| fieldValues optional | FieldValue\[\] | An listing of Field Values to be used in creating the Credential.<br>These values will be ignored if the encodedCredential is specified.<br>The id and value are required for specifying the credential fields.<br>Each credentialFormat uses a different set of Credential Fields even if they share the same name.<br>If creating a credential of type "Swipe To Enroll" the encodedCredential must match the exact length expected to come from the reader when converted from hexadecimal to binary. |
| credentialUsedWithOfflineLocks optional | Boolean | Field which specifies if the newly created credential is usable with offline locks. |

- [Request-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Credential-CreateCredential-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
       "credentialFormat" : {
                             "id" : 100
                            },
       "referenceId"      : "329",
       "encodedCredential": "28c0293",
       "fieldValues"      : [{\
                              "id"   : 121,\
                              "value": "329"\
                             },\
                             {\
                              "id"   : 212,\
                              "value": "70"\
                             }],
       "credentialUsedWithOfflineLocks" : true
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id associated with the access point |
| credentialFormat | CredentialFormat | The format of the credential<br>- `id` : The id used to reference the credential format<br>- `name`: A description of the credential format |
| referenceId | Text | A custom label or the card number. |
| encodedCredential | Text | The hexadecimal representation of this credential. |
| fieldValues | CredentialFieldValue\[\] | The list of field values which are valid for this credential.<br>- `id` : The id used to reference the credential field<br>- `value`: The value assigned for this credential<br>- `name` : The name associated with the credential field |
| size | Number | The number of bits that credentials is composed of. |
| accountId | Number | The Account Id that this credential belongs to. |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Credential-CreateCredential-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "id"               : 38981,
    "credentialFormat" : {
                          "id": 100,
                          "name": "HID 26 bit Card"
                         },
    "referenceId"      : "329",
    "encodedCredential": "28c0293",
    "fieldValues"      : [{\
                           "id"   : 1,\
                           "value": "329",\
                           "name" : "acs.cards.format.card_number"\
                          },\
                          {\
                           "id"   : 2,\
                           "value": "70",\
                           "name" : "acs.cards.format.facility_code"\
                          }],
    "size"             : 26,
    "accountId"        : 50122
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Credential-CreateCredential-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

# Credential - Create New EEN License Plate Credential

Creates an Eagle Eye Networks license plate credential and assigns it to a User. When assigning the Credential to a User, the effective date range that the credential is valid for use will also be set.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/credentials/createAndAssignEELPRCredential/{userId}
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| userId | number | id associated with the user |

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Credential optional | json | contains fields below |

## Parameter

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| referenceId | Text | The display or external value of the credential. |
| effectiveFrom optional | Date | The start date |
| effectiveTo optional | Date | The end date |

- [Request-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Credential-createAndAssignEELPRLicensePlate-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
       "referenceId"  : "TM89PAM",
       "effectiveFrom": "2023-10-13T06:11:44.789Z",
       "effectiveTo"  : "2025-12-31T12:11:44.789Z"
}
```

- [Successful Response](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Credential-createAndAssignEELPRLicensePlate-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 204 No Content
```

# Credential - Credential Listing

Retrieve a listing of credentials which the current user has view permissions for.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/credentials
```

- [Filter-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#examples-Credential-ListCredentials-0_0_0-0)

```text
/credentials?filter=reference_id__eq:12345
```

## ?QueryParam

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | Number | The offset of values before returning the first result. |
| pageSize optional | Number | The number of records to return in a Page. |
| filter optional | Text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are<br>- `status`<br>  - Filters based on a credential's status<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any credential that falls under the corresponding status<br>  - Allowed status values<br>    - assigned: returns credentials that are assigned to a user.<br>    - unassigned: returns the credentials that are not assigned.<br>- `reference_id`<br>  - Filters based on a reference id<br>  - Allowed operators:<br>    - eq: includes any credential with a reference id that contains the provided reference\_id value<br>- `facility_code`<br>  - Filters based on a facility code<br>  - Allowed operators:<br>    - eq: includes any credential with a facility code that contains the provided facility\_code value |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | Credential\[\] | Listing of Credential Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |
| count | Number | Total count of results available for criteria |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Credential-ListCredentials-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
 "offset"  : 0,
 "pageSize": 20,
 "count"   : 1,
 "data"    : [{\
                "id": 38981,\
                "credentialFormat" : {\
                                      "id"  : 100,\
                                      "name": "HID 26 bit Card"\
                                     },\
                "referenceId"      : "329",\
                "encodedCredential": "28c0293",\
                "fieldValues"      : [{\
                                       "value": "329",\
                                       "id"   : 1,\
                                       "name" : "acs.cards.format.card_number"\
                                      },\
                                      {\
                                       "value": "70",\
                                       "id"   : 2,\
                                       "name" : "acs.cards.format.facility_code"\
                                      }],\
                "size"             : 26,\
                "accountId"        : 50122\
                }]
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Credential-ListCredentials-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

# Credential - Edit Dates for Faceprint Credential

Edit the faceprint credential dates associated to the user

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/credentials/updateFaceprintCredentialDates/{userId}
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| userId | number | associated with the user |

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| EffectiveDateRange optional | json | Date range where a user's credential is enabled for use. The request body may consist of<br>- `effectiveFrom`<br>  - The starting time when a user's credential will begin to be valid.<br>- `effectiveTo`<br>  - The ending time, after which a user's credential will no longer be valid.<br>Both of the values are optional.<br>If no values are specified and the credential is already assigned to the user, no changes will be made.<br>If no values are specified and the credential is not currently assigned to the user, the effectiveFrom date will default to the current time and the effectiveTo will be left empty.<br>If only an effectiveTo date is provided, the effectiveFrom will be set to the existing effectiveFrom or to the current time if the credential was not previously assigned to the user. |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Credential-PutCredentialsUpdatefaceprintcredentialdatesUserid-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "effectiveFrom" : "2015-06-01T17:00:00Z",
  "effectiveTo"   : "2016-07-31T17:00:00Z"
}
```

- [Successful Response](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Credential-PutCredentialsUpdatefaceprintcredentialdatesUserid-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 200 No Content
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |

- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Credential-PutCredentialsUpdatefaceprintcredentialdatesUserid-0_0_0-0)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Credential-PutCredentialsUpdatefaceprintcredentialdatesUserid-0_0_0-1)

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

# Current Date Time

# Current\_Date\_Time - Get server date and time

Get current date and time from server .

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/time
```

## Header

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| current-date | Date | Current date and time in ISO 8601 format that a user must send as a part of the request ( **required**). |

- [Header-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#header-examples-Current_Date_Time-GetCurrentTime-0_0_0-0)

```json
"current-date": "2018-01-19T19:53:30.732Z"
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| time | String | current server's date and time in ISO 8601 format |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Current_Date_Time-GetCurrentTime-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
     "time": "2018-01-18T16:53:21.820Z"
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Missing current-date request-header/current-date request-header missing a value |

- [Error-Response](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Current_Date_Time-GetCurrentTime-0_0_0-0)
- [Error-Response](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Current_Date_Time-GetCurrentTime-0_0_0-1)

```json
{
     "message": "Missing request header 'current-date' for method parameter of type Date",
     "code": 400
}
```

```json
{
     "message": "Invalid current-date header value. Please provide a valid ISO 8601 date for the current-date header",
     "code": 400
}
```

# Custom Field

# Custom\_Field - Create Custom Field

Creates a new custom field definition

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/custom-fields
```

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| fieldType | Text | The type of the CustomField; TEXT, NUMBER, or DATE |
| fieldName | Text | The name of the CustomField |
| displayOrder | Number | (Optional) The order that Access will display the CustomField |
| pattern | Text | Date pattern used to parse and display values submitted for Date type custom fields. Date pattern is represented by the following characters. Increasing the number of a particular letter changes the display of the field value. Please note that the display of the examples below represents what will need to be entered in Access or the api for these values.<br>- M - Month of the year<br>- d - Day of the Month<br>- y - Year<br>Examples for January 25 2025:<br>- `MM/dd/yyyy` \- 1/25/2025<br>- `dd/MM/yyyy` \- 25/1/2025<br>- `MM-dd-yyyy` \- 1-25-2025 |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Custom_Field-CreateCustomField-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
"fieldName": "Hire Date",
"fieldType": "DATE",
"displayOrder": "1",
"pattern": "mm/dd/yyyy"
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id of the CustomField |
| fieldName | Text | The name of the CustomField |
| fieldType | Text | The type of the CustomField; TEXT, NUMBER, or DATE |
| displayOrder | Number | The order that Access will display the CustomField |
| datePattern | Text | Date pattern used to parse and display values submitted for Date type custom fields. |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Custom_Field-CreateCustomField-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "id": 2562,
    "fieldName": "Hire Date",
    "fieldType": "DATE",
    "displayOrder": "1",
    "pattern": "MM/dd/yyyy"
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 404 | Not Found, the custom field was not found |
| 400 | Bad Request, missing required values |

- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Custom_Field-CreateCustomField-0_0_0-0)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Custom_Field-CreateCustomField-0_0_0-1)

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Conflict
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message": "Unknown custom field requested for update"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
    "code"    : 400,
    "message" : "Required request parameters for custom fields were not supplied"
}
```

# Custom\_Field - Custom Field Listing

Retrieve a listing of custom fields

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/custom-fields
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset | Number | The offset of values before returning the first result. |
| pageSize | Number | The number of records to return in a Page. |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | CustomField\[\] | Listing of CustomField Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |
| count | Number | Total count of results available for criteria |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Custom_Field-ListCustomFields-0_0_0-0)

```json
"offset"  : 0,
"pageSize": 20,
"count"   : 4,
"data"    : [{\
"id": 2562,\
"fieldName": "Department",\
"fieldType": "TEXT",\
"displayOrder": "1"\
},\
{\
"id": 2763,\
"fieldName": "ID",\
"fieldType": "NUMBER",\
"displayOrder": "2"\
},\
{\
"id": 2347,\
"fieldName": "Birth Date",\
"fieldType": "DATE",\
"displayOrder": "3",\
"pattern": "yyyy-dd-MM"\
},\
{\
"id": 2348,\
"fieldName": "Hire Date",\
"fieldType": "DATE",\
"displayOrder": "4",\
"pattern": "MM/dd/yyyy"\
}\
]
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, Invalid listing criteria specified |

- [Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Custom_Field-ListCustomFields-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
"code"    : 400,
"message" : "Invalid listing criteria provided"
}
```

# Digital\_Credentials - Digital Credential Retrieval

This endpoint returns the digital credential for the current user. It does not require a userId because in many cases the current user is not required to know their own userId. An example of this would be a Brivo Mobile Pass user.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/users/credentials/digital
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id associated with the digital credential |
| credential | Text | Digital credential |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Digital_Credentials-GetUserDigitalCredential-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 200 Success
{
 "id"             : 8675309,
 "credentialValue": "MDAwMDAwMDAwMDAwMDAwMDAwMDAwMDAwMDc2NTA5",
 "effectiveFrom"  : "2016-02-02T05:00:00Z",
 "effectiveTo"    : "2020-12-31T05:00:00Z"
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 404 | Not Found, the digital credential was not found |

- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Digital_Credentials-GetUserDigitalCredential-0_0_0-0)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Digital_Credentials-GetUserDigitalCredential-0_0_0-1)

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "Invalid user"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "Digital credential not found"
}
```

# Digital\_Invitations - Assign/revoke brivo wallet passes

Assign/revoke brivo wallet passes

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/users/credentials/brivo-wallet-pass
```

- [Filter-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#examples-Digital_Invitations-UpdateBrivoWalletPass-0_0_0-0)

```text
/users/credentials/brivo-wallet-pass?nfcEnabled=true
```

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| userId | number | id associated with the user |
| accessCredentialId | number | id associated with brivo mobile pass credential |
| referenceId | Text | Reference id for the invitation. Normally it is a user's email |

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| nfcEnabled | Boolean | Whether to enable this invitation for use with NFC. Default is false. |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Digital_Invitations-UpdateBrivoWalletPass-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
 "bmpCredentials"      : [{\
         "userId"   : 7939713,\
         "accessCredentialId": 5998211,\
         "referenceId": "test@brivo.com"\
  }]
 }
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| BMPCredentials | BMPCredential\[\] | BMPCredentials with updated field included |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Digital_Invitations-UpdateBrivoWalletPass-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
   "bmpCredentials": [\
     {\
        "userId"   : 7939713,\
        "accessCredentialId": 5998211,\
        "referenceId": "test@brivo.com"\
        "updated": true\
     }\
   ]
}
 HTTP/1.1 200 OK
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |
| 409 | Conflict, the attempted action is conflicted |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 412 | Precondition Failed, You don't have any Brivo Wallet Passes available. |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Digital_Invitations-UpdateBrivoWalletPass-0_0_0-0)
- [409 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Digital_Invitations-UpdateBrivoWalletPass-0_0_0-1)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Digital_Invitations-UpdateBrivoWalletPass-0_0_0-2)
- [412 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Digital_Invitations-UpdateBrivoWalletPass-0_0_0-3)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 409 Conflict
{
  "code"    : 409,
  "message": "There is already a pending invitation for the cardHolder. No new invitation will be generated"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 412 Precondition Failed
{
  "code"    : 412,
  "message" : "You don't have any Brivo Wallet Passes available."
}
```

# Digital\_Invitations - Cancel User Digital Invitation

Cancel a digital invitation associated with the user specified by the userId

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/users/{userId}/credentials/digital-invitations
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| userId | Number | The id associated with the user |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id associated with the digital invitation |
| referenceId | Text | Reference id for the invitation. Normally it is a user's email |
| credentialId | Number | The id associated with the credential for the invitation |
| accessCode | Text | Code used to redeem credential |
| created | DateTime | The date that a digital invitation is created |
| expiration | DateTime | The expiration date of a digital invitation |
| status | Text | The status of a digital invitation |
| nfcEnabled | Boolean | Whether the digital invitation has been enabled for use with NFC |
| cancelDate | DateTime | The date that a digital invitation was canceled |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Digital_Invitations-Cancel_user_digital_invitation-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "id": 740,
  "referenceId": "john.doe@brivo.com",
  "credentialId": 967377,
  "accessCode": "i9o7aR37",
  "created": "2016-01-25T15:41:11.920Z",
  "expiration": "2016-01-28T15:41:11.920Z",
  "status": "CANCELLED",
  "nfcEnabled": false,
  "cancelDate": "2016-01-25T17:21:04.414Z"
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 404 | Not Found, the specified user was not found |

```json
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
```

# Digital\_Invitations - List User Digital Invitations

Retrieve a listing of User Digital Invitations

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/users/{userId}/credentials/digital-invitations
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | number | Listed results will display beginning from the offset value.<br>Default value: `0` |
| pageSize optional | number | The maximum number of records that will be returned for the call starting from the offset value.<br>Default value: `20`<br>Size range: `1-100` |
| filter optional | text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are<br>- `status`<br>  - Filters based on digital invitation status<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any digital invitation that falls under the corresponding status<br>  - Allowed status values<br>    - pending: returns the listing of digital invitations which are waiting to be redeemed by the user.<br>    - redeemed: returns the listing of digital invitations which are redeemed by the user.<br>    - expired: returns the listing of digital invitations which past the expiration date but have not been redeemed.<br>    - cancelled: returns the listing of digital invitations which are cancelled by the user.<br>    - all: returns the listing of digital invitations with all the statuses above. |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | DigitalInvitation\[\] | Listing of Digital Invitation Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |
| count | Number | Total count of results available for criteria |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Digital_Invitations-ListUserDigitalInvitations-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
 "data"    : [{\
               "id"           : 791,\
               "referenceId"  : "john.doe@brivo.com",\
               "accessCode"   : "uQGg3Uyc",\
               "created"      : "2016-01-25T15:48:52Z",\
               "expiration"   : "2016-01-28T15:48:52.339Z",\
               "status"       : "EXPIRED"\
              }],
 "offset"  : 0,
 "pageSize": 20,
 "count"   : 1
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 404 | Not Found, the specified user was not found |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |

- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Digital_Invitations-ListUserDigitalInvitations-0_0_0-0)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Digital_Invitations-ListUserDigitalInvitations-0_0_0-1)

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "User not found"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid status provided"
}
```

# Emergency Scenario

# Emergency\_Scenario - Clear All Emergency scenarios

Clear all active emergency scenarios, including default full scenarios. Set all devices from your account back to their normally operating state. OBS: does not consider common devices between scenarios!

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/emergency-scenarios/clear-all
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| failedScenarios | FailedScenario\[\] | The list of scenarios which failed to clear.<br>- `scenarioOid`: The id of the scenario<br>- `name` : The name of the scenario<br>- `reason` : The reason of failure |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearAllScenarios-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "failedScenarios": [\
       {\
         "scenarioOid": 99999999,\
         "name":      "Scenario 1",\
         "reason": "Failed to clear scenario 99999999 since all the devices failed to go under NORMAL"\
       }\
    ],
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |

- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearAllScenarios-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "Administrator 552345678 does not have permission to perform Clear All Scenarios"
}
```

# Emergency\_Scenario - Clear Default Emergency Egress scenario

Clear default emergency egress scenario. If an emergency egress scenario is set as default then will clear that scenario. Else will clear default full egress scenario. Set all devices from your account from egress state back to their normally operating state.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/emergency-scenarios/default-egress/clear
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| scenarioOid | Number | The id associated with the emergency scenario |
| didAllFail | Boolean | True if all devices failed to clear |
| devicesThatDidFail | ScenarioDevice\[\] | The list of devices from the scenario which failed to clear.<br>- `deviceOid`: The id of the device<br>- `name` : The name of the device |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearDefaultEgressScenario-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "didAllFail": false,
    "devicesThatDidFail": [\
       {\
         "deviceOid": 333322,\
         "name":      "Door 1"\
       }\
    ],
    "scenarioOid": 9599012
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 400 | Bad Request, Failed to initiate scenario |

- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearDefaultEgressScenario-0_0_0-0)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearDefaultEgressScenario-0_0_0-1)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearDefaultEgressScenario-0_0_0-2)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearDefaultEgressScenario-0_0_0-3)

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Initiate Emergency Default Full scenario blocked due to too many devices: {numberOfDevicesInAccount} , max: {maxDevicesDefaultFullScenario(defaultValue: 300)}"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Failed to initiate or clear scenario {scenarioId} since all the devices failed to go under {scenarioType}"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Couldn't retrieve any devices as part of {scenarioId}"
}
```

# Emergency\_Scenario - Clear Default Emergency Lockdown scenario

Clear default emergency lockdown scenario. If an emergency lockdown scenario is set as default then will clear that scenario. Else it will clear the default full lockdown scenario. Set all of the doors from your account from lockdown state back to their normally operating state.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/emergency-scenarios/default-lockdown/clear
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| scenarioOid | Number | The id associated with the emergency scenario |
| didAllFail | Boolean | True if all devices failed to clear |
| devicesThatDidFail | ScenarioDevice\[\] | The list of devices from the scenario which failed to clear.<br>- `deviceOid`: The id of the device<br>- `name` : The name of the device |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearDefaultLockdownScenario-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "didAllFail": false,
    "devicesThatDidFail": [\
       {\
         "deviceOid": 333322,\
         "name":      "Door 1"\
       }\
    ],
    "scenarioOid": 9599012
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 400 | Bad Request, Failed to initiate scenario |

- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearDefaultLockdownScenario-0_0_0-0)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearDefaultLockdownScenario-0_0_0-1)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearDefaultLockdownScenario-0_0_0-2)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearDefaultLockdownScenario-0_0_0-3)

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Initiate Emergency Default Full scenario blocked due to too many devices: {numberOfDevicesInAccount} , max: {maxDevicesDefaultFullScenario(defaultValue: 300)}"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Failed to initiate or clear scenario {scenarioId} since all the devices failed to go under {scenarioType}"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Couldn't retrieve any devices as part of {scenarioId}"
}
```

# Emergency\_Scenario - Clear Emergency Egress scenario

Clear emergency egress scenario. Set all devices configured on a scenario from egress back to their normally operating state.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/emergency-scenarios/egress/{scenarioId}/clear
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| scenarioId | number | associated with the scenario which we want to clear |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| scenarioOid | Number | The id associated with the emergency scenario |
| didAllFail | Boolean | True if all devices failed to clear |
| devicesThatDidFail | ScenarioDevice\[\] | The list of devices from the scenario which failed to clear.<br>- `deviceOid`: The id of the device<br>- `name` : The name of the device |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearEmergencyEgressScenario-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "didAllFail": false,
    "devicesThatDidFail": [\
       {\
         "deviceOid": 333322,\
         "name":      "Door 1"\
       }\
    ],
    "scenarioOid": 9599012
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 404 | Not Found, the specified emergency scenario of that type was not found |
| 400 | Bad Request, Failed to initiate scenario |

- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearEmergencyEgressScenario-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearEmergencyEgressScenario-0_0_0-1)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearEmergencyEgressScenario-0_0_0-2)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearEmergencyEgressScenario-0_0_0-3)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-clearEmergencyEgressScenario-0_0_0-4)

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "Scenario {scenarioId} is not part of account {accountId}"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "Scenario {scenarioId} of type {scenarioType} not found"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Failed to initiate or clear scenario {scenarioId} since all the devices failed to go under {scenarioType}"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Couldn't retrieve any devices as part of {scenarioId}"
}
```

# Emergency\_Scenario - Initiate Default Emergency Egress scenario

Initiate default emergency egress scenario. If an emergency egress scenario is set as default then will initiate that scenario. Else will initiate default full egress scenario. Default Full egress scenario set all devices from your account to an emergency egress state.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/emergency-scenarios/default-egress/initiate
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| scenarioOid | Number | The id associated with the emergency scenario |
| didAllFail | Boolean | True if all devices failed to initiate |
| devicesThatDidFail | ScenarioDevice\[\] | The list of devices from the scenario which failed to initiate.<br>- `deviceOid`: The id of the device<br>- `name` : The name of the device |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Emergency_Scenario-initiateDefaultEgressScenario-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "didAllFail": false,
    "devicesThatDidFail": [\
       {\
         "deviceOid": 333322,\
         "name":      "Door 1"\
       }\
    ],
    "scenarioOid": 9599012
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 400 | Bad Request, Failed to initiate scenario |

- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-initiateDefaultEgressScenario-0_0_0-0)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-initiateDefaultEgressScenario-0_0_0-1)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-initiateDefaultEgressScenario-0_0_0-2)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-initiateDefaultEgressScenario-0_0_0-3)

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Initiate Emergency Default Full scenario blocked due to too many devices: {numberOfDevicesInAccount} , max: {maxDevicesDefaultFullScenario(defaultValue: 300)}"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Failed to initiate or clear scenario {scenarioId} since all the devices failed to go under {scenarioType}"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Couldn't retrieve any devices as part of {scenarioId}"
}
```

# Emergency\_Scenario - Initiate Default Emergency Lockdown scenario

Initiate default emergency lockdown scenario. If an emergency lockdown scenario is set as the default, then this endpoint will initiate that scenario. Else the default full lockdown scenario will be initiated. Default Full Lockdown is available on every Access account and is a scenario that sets all of the doors in your account to an emergency lockdown state.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/emergency-scenarios/default-lockdown/initiate
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| scenarioOid | Number | The id associated with the emergency scenario |
| didAllFail | Boolean | True if all devices failed to initiate |
| devicesThatDidFail | ScenarioDevice\[\] | The list of devices from the scenario which failed to initiate.<br>- `deviceOid`: The id of the device<br>- `name` : The name of the device |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Emergency_Scenario-initiateDefaultLockdownScenario-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "didAllFail": false,
    "devicesThatDidFail": [\
       {\
         "deviceOid": 333322,\
         "name":      "Door 1"\
       }\
    ],
    "scenarioOid": 9599012
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 400 | Bad Request, Failed to initiate scenario |

- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-initiateDefaultLockdownScenario-0_0_0-0)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-initiateDefaultLockdownScenario-0_0_0-1)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-initiateDefaultLockdownScenario-0_0_0-2)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Emergency_Scenario-initiateDefaultLockdownScenario-0_0_0-3)

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Initiate Emergency Default Full scenario blocked due to too many devices: {numberOfDevicesInAccount} , max: {maxDevicesDefaultFullScenario(defaultValue: 300)}"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Failed to initiate or clear scenario {scenarioId} since all the devices failed to go under {scenarioType}"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Couldn't retrieve any devices as part of {scenarioId}"
}
```

# Emergency\_Scenario - List active emergency scenarios

Retrieve a listing of all active emergency scenarios of type lockdown and egress.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/emergency-scenarios/active-scenarios
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | Number | The count of where to start the requested Page<br>Default value: `0` |
| pageSize optional | Number | The number of records to return in a Page, default size is 20 and max size is 100.<br>Default value: `20`<br>Size range: `1-100` |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | EmergencyScenario\[\] | The list of emergency scenarios<br>- `id`: The objectId of the emergency scenario,<br>- `name`: The name of the emergency scenario,<br>- `isDefault`: true/false is the emergency scenario set as default,<br>- `deviceIds`\[\]: The list of assigned devices to the emergency scenario,<br>- `triggerIds`\[\]: The list of assigned triggers to the emergency scenario,<br>- `created`: creation date of the emergency scenario,<br>- `updated`: updating date of the emergency scenario,<br>- `issued`: null or activation date when the scenario was initiated as long as it is active<br>- `threatLevelTypeId`: The type of the emergency scenario (2- LOCKDOWN, 3- Egress) |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |
| count | Number | Total count of results available for criteria |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Emergency_Scenario-getActiveEmergencyScenariosList-0_0_0-0)

```json
[\
  {\
    "id": 7020884,\
    "name": "Lockdown scenario 1",\
    "isDefault": false,\
    "deviceIds": [\
         5648473,\
         5648605,\
         ....\
    ],\
    "triggerIds": [],\
    "created": "2024-01-30T06:36:05.302Z",\
    "updated": "2024-02-05T07:19:17.940Z",\
    "issued": null,\
    "threatLevelTypeId": 2\
  },\
  {\
     "id": 7030920,\
     "name": "Egress scenario 1",\
     "isDefault": false,\
     "deviceIds": [\
                5648473,\
                5648605,\
                5648606,...\
      ],\
      "triggerIds": [],\
      "created": "2024-01-30T06:36:05.302Z",\
      "updated": "2024-02-05T07:19:17.940Z",\
      "issued": "2024-02-06T06:22:41.158Z",\
      "threatLevelTypeId": 3\
   }, ...\
],
 "offset": 0,
 "pageSize": 20,
 "count": 5
```

# Emergency\_Scenario - List emergency scenarios

Retrieve a listing of all emergency scenarios of type lockdown and egress.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/emergency-scenarios
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | Number | The count of where to start the requested Page<br>Default value: `0` |
| pageSize optional | Number | The number of records to return in a Page, default size is 20 and max size is 100.<br>Default value: `20`<br>Size range: `1-100` |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | EmergencyScenario\[\] | The list of emergency scenarios<br>- `id`: The objectId of the emergency scenario,<br>- `name`: The name of the emergency scenario,<br>- `isDefault`: true/false is the emergency scenario set as default,<br>- `deviceIds`\[\]: The list of assigned devices to the emergency scenario,<br>- `triggerIds`\[\]: The list of assigned triggers to the emergency scenario,<br>- `created`: creation date of the emergency scenario,<br>- `updated`: updating date of the emergency scenario,<br>- `issued`: null or activation date when the scenario was initiated as long as it is active<br>- `threatLevelTypeId`: The type of the emergency scenario (2- LOCKDOWN, 3- Egress) |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |
| count | Number | Total count of results available for criteria |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Emergency_Scenario-getEmergencyScenariosList-0_0_0-0)

```json
[\
  {\
    "id": 7020884,\
    "name": "Lockdown scenario 1",\
    "isDefault": false,\
    "deviceIds": [\
         5648473,\
         5648605,\
         ....\
    ],\
    "triggerIds": [],\
    "created": "2024-01-30T06:36:05.302Z",\
    "updated": "2024-02-05T07:19:17.940Z",\
    "issued": null,\
    "threatLevelTypeId": 2\
  },\
  {\
     "id": 7030920,\
     "name": "Egress scenario 1",\
     "isDefault": false,\
     "deviceIds": [\
                5648473,\
                5648605,\
                5648606,...\
      ],\
      "triggerIds": [],\
      "created": "2024-01-30T06:36:05.302Z",\
      "updated": "2024-02-05T07:19:17.940Z",\
      "issued": "2024-02-06T06:22:41.158Z",\
      "threatLevelTypeId": 3\
   }, ...\
],
 "offset": 0,
 "pageSize": 20,
 "count": 5
```

# Event Subscription

# Event\_Subscription - Create New Event Subscription

Create a new event subscription.

The event subscription defines a set of criteria for you to register a url to POST event data to. When the criteria defined for a subscription are met, a notification is sent to the url provided.

| Supported Criteria Types | Description |
| --- | --- |
| SITE | Filters on site id |
| USER | Filters on user id |
| ACCESS-POINT | Filters on device id |
| AUDIT | Filters to audit events (1) or access events (0, default) |

Audit events (or Journal events) are those listed in the [audit events endpoint](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#api-Events-ListAuditEvent) and the Access Journal page. Access events are those listed in the [access events endpoint](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#api-Events-ListAccessEvent) and displayed in the Access Event Tracker page.

| Supported Criteria Operation Types | Description |
| --- | --- |
| EQ | Equal |
| NE | Not Equal |

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/event-subscriptions
```

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| name | Text | The Name of the event subscription. |
| url | Text | A listening url that will receive the POST notification messages for this event subscription |
| errorEmail | Text | E-mail address that will be notified in the case that there was a failure sending the notification. |
| criteria | EventSubscriptionCriteria\[\] | A set of event subscription criteria to match against.<br>The criteria parameters act as an AND condition. All criteria parameters must be met for the event subscription to trigger.<br>Multiple conflicting criteria such as using EQ operations on two different sites will never trigger an event subscription |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Event_Subscription-EventSubscription-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "name" : "Site 1",
  "url" : "http://requestb.in/13755vw1",
  "errorEmail": "john.doe@acme.com",
  "criteria": [\
                  {\
                    "criteriaType": "SITE",\
                    "criteriaOperationType": "EQ",\
                    "criteriaValue": 12345\
                  },\
                  {\
                    "criteriaType": "USER",\
                    "criteriaOperationType": "NE",\
                    "criteriaValue": 23361\
                  }\
              ]
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The ID assigned to the event subscription. |
| name | Text | The Name of the event subscription. |
| url | Text | The url event subscription goes to. |
| errorEmail | Text | Email address to send a failure to post notification to |
| criteria | EventSubscriptionCriteria\[\] | Event subscription criteria |
| encryptedSecretWord | Text | The Brivo secret word encrypted with the client Id (without the dashes). Using 'AES/CBC/NoPadding' encryption scheme. |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Event_Subscription-EventSubscription-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "id" : 2452345,
  "name" : "Site 1",
  "url" : "http://requestb.in/13755vw1",
  "errorEmail": "john.doe@acme.com",
  "criteria": [\
                  {\
                    "id": 349,\
                    "criteriaType": "SITE",\
                    "criteriaOperationType": "EQ",\
                    "criteriaValue": 12345\
                  },\
                  {\
                    "id": 350,\
                    "criteriaType": "USER",\
                    "criteriaOperationType": "NE",\
                    "criteriaValue": 23361\
                  }\
              ],
              "encryptedSecretWord": "rL6NGWa1TkxGsyl3M3Fp9w=="
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, Invalid Site criteria |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Event_Subscription-EventSubscription-0_0_0-0)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Event_Subscription-EventSubscription-0_0_0-1)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Event_Subscription-EventSubscription-0_0_0-2)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Event_Subscription-EventSubscription-0_0_0-3)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Event subscription contained invalid Site criteria"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Event subscription contained invalid Device criteria"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

# Event\_Subscription - Event Subscription Listing

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/event-subscriptions
```

## ?QueryParam

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | number | The offset of values before returning the first result.<br>Default value: `0` |
| pageSize optional | number | The number of records to return in a Page.<br>Default value: `20`<br>Size range: `1-100` |
| filter optional | Text | The filter parameter for passing in optional filter criteria. Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are<br>- `name`<br>  - Filters based on the event subscription name<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any event subscription with the name provided |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | EventSubscription\[\] | Listing of EventSubscription Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |
| count | Number | Total count of results available for criteria |

```json
 "pageSize": 20,
 "count"   : 2,
 "data"    : [\
              {\
                "id": 227,\
                "name": "John's Desk - Primary Door",\
                "url": "http://johndoe/event/site/door",\
                "errorEmail": "john.doe@brivo.com",\
                "criteria": [\
                  {\
                    "id": 349,\
                    "criteriaType": "USER",\
                    "criteriaOperationType": "NE",\
                    "criteriaValue": 23361\
                  },\
                  {\
                    "id": 348,\
                    "criteriaType": "ACCESS-POINT",\
                    "criteriaOperationType": "EQ",\
                    "criteriaValue": 24167\
                  }\
                ]\
              },\
              {\
                "id": 271,\
                "name": "motionDetection",\
                "url": "http://johndoe/event/motion",\
```

# Events

# Events - Access Events Count

Retrieve a Count of Access Events. Access events include Camera, Panel, and User Events.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/events/counts/access
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| filter optional | text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are<br>- `occurred`<br>  - Filter based on the time the event occurred<br>  - By default occurred is limited to the current day starting at midnight UTC.<br>  - An occurred range cannot be longer than a 24 hour period.<br>  - The occurred times are truncated to the nearest hour.<br>  - A smaller range can be searched by specifying an offset from the end.<br>  - In order to page through the events specify the offset as the last occurred time of the current page.<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - gt: Searches for events after a specified date and time value<br>    - lt: Searches for events before a specified date and time value<br>  - Both a GT and LT filter can be used by applying the separator (;) as described in the [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters)<br>- `object`<br>  - Any valid device, access-point, camera, or control panel id.<br>  - May not be combined with Site filter.<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Returns events that have the provided object id value<br>- `site`<br>  - Filter based on the site id value<br>  - May not be combined with object filter.<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Returns events that have the provided site id value<br>- `event_type`<br>  - Filter of event types which are desired<br>  - Supports multiple comma separated values<br>  - Default value is all valid Event Types.<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Returns events which fall into one of the specified types.<br>  - Valid Access Event Types:<br>    - non\_exception<br>    - exception<br>    - camera<br>    - video\_linkable |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| EventCount | EventCount | result with specified criteria |

- [Success-Response](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Events-AccessEventCount-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
 "count": 0
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, Invalid criteria were provided for the listing call |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Events-AccessEventCount-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Events-AccessEventCount-0_0_0-1)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
 "code"    : 400,
 "message" : "Invalid count criteria provided"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

# Events - Access Events Listing

Retrieve a listing of Access Events. Access events include Camera, Panel, and User Events. Events are ordered naturally from most recent to oldest. In order to retrieve a count for the events use the /events/counts/access Call.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/events/access
```

- [Filter-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#examples-Events-ListAccessEvent-0_0_0-0)

```text
/events/access?offset=2019-09-16T20:00:00Z&pageSize=100&filter=occurred__gt:2019-09-16T00:00:00Z
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | date | Listed results will display beginning from the offset value. If specified the offset for event listings should be the minimum occurred value of the last page read. |
| pageSize optional | number | The maximum number of records that will be returned for the call starting from the offset value.<br>Size range: `1-100` |
| filter optional | text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are<br>- `occurred`<br>  - Filter based on the time the event occurred<br>  - By default occurred is limited to the current day starting at midnight UTC.<br>  - An occurred range cannot be longer than a 24 hour period.<br>  - The occurred times are truncated to the nearest hour.<br>  - A smaller range can be searched by specifying an offset from the end.<br>  - In order to page through the events specify the offset as the last occurred time of the current page.<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - gt: Searches for events after a specified date and time value<br>    - lt: Searches for events before a specified date and time value<br>  - Both a GT and LT filter can be used by applying the separator (;) as described in the [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters)<br>- `object`<br>  - Any valid device, access-point, camera, or control panel id.<br>  - May not be combined with Site filter.<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Returns events that have the provided object id value<br>- `site`<br>  - Filter based on the site id value<br>  - May not be combined with object filter.<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Returns events that have the provided site id value<br>- `event_type`<br>  - Filter of event types which are desired<br>  - Supports multiple comma separated values<br>  - Default value is all valid Event Types.<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Returns events which fall into one of the specified types.<br>  - Valid Access Event Types:<br>    - non\_exception<br>    - exception<br>    - camera |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | Event\[\] | Listing of Event Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |

- [Success-Response](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Events-ListAccessEvent-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "data": [\
       {\
           "uuid": "049e1ca7-592a-4249-8f8c-ebcdc8e28594",\
           "securityAction": {\
               "securityActionId": 5064,\
               "action": "Administrator Pulse Output",\
               "exception": false\
           },\
           "actor": {\
               "id": 912347,\
               "name": "QA Admin"\
           },\
           "eventObject": {\
               "id": 408023598,\
               "name": "Door 1",\

                   "name": "Door"\
```
