# Events - Audit Events Count

Retrieve a Count of the number of audit events over a time period. This function accepts the same parameters as the listing call except for offset and pageSize and will return the number of Events matching the filter criteria of a Listing call.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/events/counts/audit
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| filter optional | text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are<br>- `occurred`<br>  - Count based on the time the event occurred<br>  - By default occurred is limited to the current day starting at midnight UTC.<br>  - An occurred range cannot be longer than a 24 hour period.<br>  - The occurred times are truncated to the nearest hour.<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Searches for events on the day specified, disregarding the time values<br>    - gt: Searches for events after a specified date and time value<br>    - lt: Searches for events before a specified date and time value<br>  - Both a GT and LT filter can be used by applying the separator (;) as described in the [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters)<br>- `actor`<br>  - Count based on the actor id value<br>  - May not be combined with object criteria.<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Returns events that have the provided actor id value<br>- `object`<br>  - Count based on the object id value<br>  - May not be combined with actor criteria<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Returns events that have the provided object id value<br>- `schedule`<br>  - Filter based on the schedule id value<br>  - May not be combined with actor, object, or holiday criteria<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Returns events that have the provided schedule id value<br>- `holiday`<br>  - Filter based on the holiday id value<br>  - May not be combined with actor, object, or schedule criteria<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Returns events that have the provided holiday id value<br>- `event_type`<br>  - Count only event types which are specified<br>  - Supports multiple comma separated values<br>  - Default value includes all event types.<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Returns events which fall into one of the specified types.<br>  - Valid Audit Event types are:<br>    - account<br>    - administrator<br>    - badge<br>    - control\_panel<br>    - credential<br>    - custom\_field<br>    - device<br>    - group<br>    - holiday<br>    - ipac<br>    - notification<br>    - permission\_template<br>    - report<br>    - schedule<br>    - site<br>    - user<br>    - video |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| EventCount | EventCount | result with specified criteria |

- [Success-Response](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Events-CountAuditEvent-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
 "count": 0
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, Invalid criteria were provided for the listing call |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Events-CountAuditEvent-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Events-CountAuditEvent-0_0_0-1)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
 "code"    : 400,
 "message" : "Invalid count criteria provided"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

# Events - Audit Events Listing

Retrieve a listing of Audit Events. The Audit Event listing includes any actions that are taken by an Administor. This API provides the same functionality as the Brivo Access Journal. In order to retrieve a count for the events use the /events/counts/audit Call.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/events/audit
```

- [Filter-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#examples-Events-ListAuditEvent-0_0_0-0)

```text
/events/audit?offset=2019-09-16T20:00:00Z&pageSize=100&filter=occurred__gt:2019-09-16T00:00:00Z
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | date | Listed results will display beginning from the offset value. If specified the offset for event listings should be the minimum occurred value of the last page read. |
| pageSize optional | number | The maximum number of records that will be returned for the call starting from the offset value.<br>Size range: `1-100` |
| filter optional | text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are<br>- `occurred`<br>  - Filter based on the time the event occurred<br>  - By default occurred is limited to the current day starting at midnight UTC.<br>  - An occurred range cannot be longer than a 24 hour period.<br>  - The occurred times are truncated to the nearest hour.<br>  - A smaller range can be searched by specifying an offset from the end.<br>  - In order to page through the events specify the offset as the last occurred time of the current page.<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - gt: Searches for events after a specified date and time value<br>    - lt: Searches for events before a specified date and time value<br>  - Both a GT and LT filter can be used by applying the separator (;) as described in the [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters)<br>- `actor`<br>  - Filter based on the actor id value<br>  - May not be combined with object criteria.<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Returns events that have the provided actor id value<br>- `object`<br>  - Filter based on the object id value<br>  - May not be combined with actor criteria<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Returns events that have the provided object id value<br>- `schedule`<br>  - Filter based on the schedule id value<br>  - May not be combined with actor, object, or holiday criteria<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Returns events that have the provided schedule id value<br>- `holiday`<br>  - Filter based on the holiday id value<br>  - May not be combined with actor, object, or schedule criteria<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Returns events that have the provided holiday id value<br>- `event_type`<br>  - Filter of event types which are desired<br>  - Supports multiple comma separated values<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Returns events which fall into one of the specified types.<br>  - Valid Audit Event types are:<br>    - account<br>    - administrator<br>    - badge<br>    - control\_panel<br>    - credential<br>    - custom\_field<br>    - device<br>    - group<br>    - holiday<br>    - ipac<br>    - notification<br>    - permission\_template<br>    - report<br>    - schedule<br>    - site<br>    - user<br>    - video |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | Event\[\] | Listing of Event Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |

- [Success-Response](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Events-ListAuditEvent-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "data": [\
       {\
           "uuid": "049e1ca7-592a-4249-8f8c-ebcdc8e28594",\
           "securityAction": {\
               "securityActionId": 3005,\
               "action": "User Login",\
               "exception": false\
           },\
           "actor": {\
               "id": 912347,\
               "name": "QA Admin"\
           },\
           "occurred": "2024-04-17T08:52:39.724Z",\
           "processed": "2024-04-17T08:52:39.726Z",\
           "eventData": {\
               "actorName": "QA Admin",\
               "objectTypeId": 0\
           }\
       }\
   ],
   "pageSize": 20
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, Invalid criteria were provided for the listing call |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Events-ListAuditEvent-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Events-ListAuditEvent-0_0_0-1)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
 "code"    : 400,
 "message" : "Invalid listing criteria provided"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

# Events - Event json structure

The json structure for an event returned by a triggered event-subscription

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/events/...
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| uuid | UUID | The event id of the security event object. |
| securityAction | SecurityAction | A description of the type of the event. |
| securityActionId | Number | The event type id associated to this event. |
| action | Text | A description of the event. |
| exception | Boolean | Whether or not this event is considered an exception or normal behavior. |
| actor | ApiObject | The acting object for the event. Generally a User or an Administrator. |
| id | Number | The id of the actor. |
| objectType | Text | The API object type for the actor. |
| name | Text | The actor's name, when applicable. |
| email | Text | The actor's email, when applicable. |
| impersonator | ApiObject | The information of the parent authentication if the action was performed via remote login. This will generally be null. |
| id | Number | The impersonating administrator's id. |
| name | Text | The name of the impersonating administrator. |
| eventObject | ApiObject | The API object that was acted on, often an access-point. |
| id | Number | The id of the associated object. |
| objectType | Text | The type of the API object. |
| name | Text | The name of the API object. |
| site | Site | The site that the event occurred at. |
| id | Number | The id of the Site for this event. |
| siteName | Text | The name of the site. |
| occurred | DateTime | The time that the event occurred at. |
| eventData | EventData | Associated event attributes which give context to some events. |
| actorUserTypeId | Number | The User type of the actor making the changes. |
| objectGroupName | Text | The name of the object group being affected. |
| actionAllowed | Boolean | If the action is allowed. |
| numericValue | Number |  |
| unknownWeigand | Text | The Weigand value of an unkown card , in hex. |
| objectSubtypeId | Number | The subtype id of the object, if applicable. |
| userTypeId | Number | The user type of the affected user. |
| objectTypeId | Number | The type of the affected object. |
| impersonatorObjectId | Number | Set when a RunAs token is being used to make changes. |
| impersonatorName | Text | Set when a RunAs token is being used to make changes. |
| impersonatorUserTypeId | Number | Set when a RunAs token is being used to make changes. |
| detail | Text | An optional description of the event. |
| securityActionIdPermission | Number | For use with 500 and 501 events. |
| privilegeTargetName | Text | For use with 500 and 501 events. |
| firstCardNumber | Number | For use with 1007 and 1008 events. |
| lastCardNumber | Number | For use with 1007 and 1008 events. |
| facilityCode | Number | For use with 1007 and 1008 events. |
| systemCode | Number | For use with 1007 and 1008 events. |
| agencyCode | Number | For use with 1007 and 1008 events. |
| siteCode | Number | For use with 1007 and 1008 events. |
| credentialSeries | Text | For use with 1007 and 1008 events. |
| individualCredentialIssue | Text | For use with 1007 and 1008 events. |
| personIdentifier | Text | For use with 1007 and 1008 events. |
| organizationalIdentifier | Text | For use with 1007 and 1008 events. |
| organizationAssociationCategory | Text | For use with 1007 and 1008 events. |
| credentialsFoundInRange | Number | Used with the 1008 event. |
| credentialsDeleted | Number | Used with the 1008 event. |
| credentialLabel | Text | Used with the 1007 , 1008 , 3004 , 5012 , 5013 , 5014 , 5017 , 5018 , 5034 , 5065 events. |
| credentialTypeId | Number | Used with the 1007 , 1008 , 3004 , 5012 , 5013 , 5014 , 5017 , 5018 , 5034 , 5065 events. |
| credentialType | Test | Used with the 1007 , 1008 , 3004 , 5012 , 5013 , 5014 , 5017 , 5018 , 5034 , 5065 events. |
| credentialObjectId | Number | Used with the 5016 event. |
| deviceTypeId | Number | Used with 2002 , ... events. |
| siteName | Number | Used with 4101 , 4102 , 4103 , 4104 events. |
| siteObjectId | Number | Used with 4101 , 4102 , 4103 , 4104 events. |
| userGroupName | Text | Used with 4001 , 4002 , 4003 , 4004 events. |
| userGroupObjectId | Number | Used with 4001 , 4002 , 4003 , 4004 events. |
| userId | Text | Used with 6201 , 6202 events. |
| controlPanelNumber | Text | Used with 6201 , 6202 events. |
| badgeTemplateName | Text | Used with the 7404 event type. |
| badgeTemplateId | Number |  |
| reportJobId | Number | Used with 7509 event. |
| adminFullName | Text | Used with 7703 and 7704 events. |
| userDefinedMessage | Text | Used with 5019 , 5020 , 5037 , 5038 events. Timer , Switch , device custom messages. |
| batteryLevel | Number | Used with the 5023 event. |
| boardNumber | Number | Used with the 5039 , 5040 , 5041 , 5042 , 5043 , 5044 , 5045 , 5046 , 5047 , 5048 , 5049 events. |
| boardPointNumber | Number | Used with the 5039 , 5040 , 5041 , 5042 , 5043 , 5044 , 5045 , 5046 , 5047 , 5048 , 5049 events. |
| boardTypeId | Number | Used with the 5039 , 5040 , 5041 , 5042 , 5043 , 5044 , 5045 , 5046 , 5047 , 5048 , 5049 events. |
| scheduleName | Text | Sent with 5055 , 500 , and 501 events. |
| scheduleObjectId | Number | Sent with 5055 event. |
| saltoFirmwareNumber | Text | Sent with 5202 events. |
| saltoFirmwareVersion | Text | Sent with 5202 events. |
| saltoManufacturedTime | Number | Sent with 5202 events. |
| saltoNodeAddress | Text | This is a hex value sent with 5211 and 5212 events. |
| panelTypeId | Number | The type of a Panel For use with 6201 and 6202 events. |
| credentialBitLength | Number | Used with the 5012 event. |
| failedConversion | Boolean | Used with the 5012 event. |
| brainTypeId | Number | The ID of a panel. |
| securityGroupTypeId | Number | Site or User Group ID. |
| secondFactorCredentialOid | Number | Set for 5058 events. |
| propertyChanges | ChangeSet | A list of property changes for altered domain objects. |
| property | Text | The name of the property which changed. |
| previousValue | Text | The previous value of the property , omitted if the property was previously not set. |
| currentValue | Text | The current value of the property , omitted if the property is null. |
| credentials | Credential | One or more credentials associated with the Event. |
| id | Number | The ID of the credential if it is known. |
| reference\_id | Text | The value presented if the credential is not known. |

- [Event model](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Events-EventModel-0_0_0-0)

```json
 {
    "objectType": "ACCESS_POINT",
    "uuid": "ae217d80-f38b-4521-aaaa-c3b84e763552",
    "securityAction": {
      "securityActionId": 5064,
      "action": "Administrator Pulse Output",
      "exception": false
    },
    "actor": {
      "id": 10457058,

      }

      "siteName": "Home base"
    },

    "actorName": "qa admin",
    "actorUserTypeId": 1,
```

# Features

# Features - Get Features

Retrieves the list of features for given user's account

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/features
```

Permission:
None


## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| features | Object\[\] | Array of feature objects |
| id | Number | The ID assigned to the feature |
| key | String | The feature key |
| displayOrder | Number | Display order of the feature |
| applicationId | Number | The application ID associated with the feature |
| permissionSet | String | The permission set for the feature |
| permissions | Object\[\] | Array of permission objects |
| id | Number | The permission ID |
| key | String | The permission key |
| limited | Boolean | Whether the permission is limited |
| hasPermission | Boolean | Whether the user has this permission |
| dependencies | Number\[\] | Array of permission dependency IDs |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Features-GetFeatures-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 200 OK
[\
  {\
    "id": 0,\
    "key": "string",\
    "displayOrder": 0,\
    "applicationId": 0,\
    "permissionSet": "string",\
    "permissions": [\
      {\
        "id": 0,\
        "key": "string",\
        "limited": true,\
        "hasPermission": true,\
        "dependencies": [0]\
      }\
    ],\
    "externalFeatureFlag": "string"\
  }\
]
```

# Group - Assign Permission to Group

Assign a group permission to the given accessPoint

\- This action is only available to Brivo Account Config Tool Administrators

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/groups/{groupId}/access/access-points/{accessPointId}
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| accessPointId | number | The id associated with the accesspoint |
| groupId | number | The id associated with the group |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Group-assignPermissionToGroup-0_0_0-0)

```json
 AccessPermission
{
    "schedule": {
        "id": 439955
    },
    "privacyModeOverride": true
}
```

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Group-assignPermissionToGroup-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
"accessPoint": {
"id": 442211,
"name": "Wireless Revolving Door"
"type": "Salto Door"
},
"schedule": {
"id": 439955,
"name": "24x7 - Always On"
},
"privacyModeOverride": true
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |
| 404 | Not Found, the access point specified does not exist or is not accessible |
| 403 | Forbidden, You are not allowed to perform that action |

# Group - Delete Group

Deletes the group associated with the provided id

\- This action is only available to Brivo Account Config Tool Administrators

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/groups/{groupId}
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| groupId | number | The id associated with the group |

- [Success example](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Group-DeleteGroup-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 204 No Content
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |

| 404 | Not Found, the specified group was not found |

- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Group-DeleteGroup-0_0_0-1)

# Group - Group Listing

Retrieve a listing of Groups

\- This action is only available to Brivo Account Config Tool Administrators

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/groups
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | number | Listed results will display beginning from the offset value. |
| pageSize optional | number | The maximum number of records that will be returned for the call starting from the offset value.<br>Size range: `1-100` |
| filter optional | text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are: - \`name\` - Filters based on a group name - Allowed operators: - eq: includes any group with a name that contains the provided name value |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | Group\[\] | Listing of Group Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |

```json
"name"   : "Staff"\
}],
"offset"  : 0,
"pageSize": 20,
"count"   : 1
}
```

```json
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
```
```json
}
```

# Group - List Group Permission

Retrieve a listing of access points and schedules that belong to the specified group.

\- This action is only available to Brivo Account Config Tool Administrators

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/groups/{groupId}/access/access-points
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | Number | Listed results will display beginning from the offset value. |
| pageSize optional | Number | The maximum number of records that will be returned for the call starting from the offset value.<br>Size range: `1-100` |
| filter optional | text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are: - \`access\_point\_name\` - Filters based on a access point name - Allowed operators: - eq: includes any access point with access point name that contains the provided access point name value <br>\- \`access\_point\_type\` - Filters based on a access point type - Multiple values can be comma separated - Allowed operators: - eq: includes any access point with a given access point type value - ne: excludes any access point with a given access point type value - Allowed access\_point\_type values - DOOR - WIEGAND - FLOOR - SALTO\_DOOR - ALLEGION\_DOOR - ASSA\_ABLOY\_DOOR - returns access points that match the given access point type value. - \`schedule\_name\` - Filters based on a schedule\_name name - Allowed operators: - eq: includes any schedule with schedule name that contains the provided name value <br>\- \`privacy\_mode\_override\` - Filters based on a privacy\_mode\_override - Allowed operators: - eq: includes any privacy mode override with the given privacy mode override value - Allowed privacy\_mode\_override values - TRUE, FALSE - returns access points that match the given privacy mode override value. - \`Note:\` privacy mode is currently supported only for Salto, Allegion and ASSA Abloy access point types |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | data\[\] | Listing of AccessPermission Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |
| count | Number | Total count of results available for criteria |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Group-GetGroupsGroupidAccessAccessPoints-0_0_0-0)

```json
AccessPermission[]
{
"data": [\
{\
"accessPoint": {\
"id": 442211,\
"name": "Revolving Door",\
"type": "Allegion Door"\
<p>\
},\
"schedule": {\
"id": 339955,\
"name": "24x7 - Always On"\
}\
},\
{\
"accessPoint": {\
"id": 58805,\
"name": "Sample salto door",\
"type": "Salto Door Lock"\
},\
"schedule": {\

"name": "24x7 Schedule"\
},\
"privacyModeOverride": true\
},\
{\

"name": "salto_sample_door",\
"type": "Salto Door Lock"\
},\
"schedule": {\
"id": 43293,\
"name": "24x7 Schedule"\
}\
},\
{\
"accessPoint": {\
"id": 542211,\
"name": "Security Door",\
"type": "Door"\
<p>\
},\
"schedule": {\
"id": 439955,\
"name": "9 to 5 - Sometimes On"\
},\
}\
],
"offset": 0,
"pageSize": 20,
"count": 4
}
```

# Group - Update Group

Update the group associated with the provided id

\- This action is only available to Brivo Account Config Tool Administrators

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/groups/{groupId}
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| groupId | number | The id associated with the group |

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| name | Text | Group name |
| keypadUnlock optional | boolean | The keypad unlock state for this group |
| immuneToAntipassback optional | boolean | The immune to passback setting |
| excludedFromLockdown optional | boolean | The excluded for lockdown setting |
| antipassbackResetTime optional | Text | The antipassback reset time - this is send as an integer representing the minute in the day for the specified time - between 0 and 1440 . Setting an empty string will clear the value |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Group-UpdateGroup-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "name"                 : "Staff",
  "keypadUnlock"         : true,
  "immuneToAntipassback" : true,
  "excludedFromLockdown" : true,
  "antipassbackResetTime": "1399"
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id associated with the Group |
| name | Text | The name of the group |
| antipassbackResetTime | Number | The Antipassback reset time value in 24 hour time format |
| keypadUnlock | Boolean | The ability to unlock keypads |
| immuneToAntipassback | Boolean | Immunity to Antipassback |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Group-UpdateGroup-0_0_0-0)

```json

{
    "id"     : 76336,
    "name"   : "Staff",
    "antipassbackResetTime" : "23:59",
    "keypadUnlock" : false,
    "immuneToAntipassback" : false
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 404 | Not Found, the specified group was not found |

- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Group-UpdateGroup-0_0_0-0)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Group-UpdateGroup-0_0_0-1)

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "Group not found"
```

# Guest

# Guest - Create new Guest by Admin host

Create a new Guest by Admin host

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/brivo-visitor/create-and-assign-visitor-user
```

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| user | json | User data of the Guest. The request body may consist of<br>- `firstName`<br>  - Guest's first name.<br>- `effectiveFrom`<br>  - The beginning date that a Guest's PIN is valid for use.<br>- `effectiveTo`<br>  - The beginning date that a Guest's PIN is valid for use.<br>- `emails`<br>  - Array of Email objects associated with this Guest. Email has address and type.<br>All fields are mandatory. |
| groupIds | Number\[\] | Array of Groups oids where the guest will have permissions. |
| credentialType optional | Text | The type of the guest credential. Can be "PIN" or "MOBILE\_PASS". If this field is missing, the default is "PIN". If "MOBILE\_PASS" is provided, the Guest will have a Brivo Mobile Pass associated. |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Guest-CreateAndAssignGuestUser-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "user": {
        "firstName": "guest 5 by admin",
        "effectiveFrom": "2024-11-11T10:18:50.549Z",
        "effectiveTo": "2024-11-30T15:18:00Z",
        "emails": [{"address":"cv@brivo.com", "type":"work"}]
    },
    "groupIds": [\
        11906589,\
        11906588\
    ],
    "credentialType": "MOBILE_PASS"
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id associated with the user (Guest) |
| firstName | Text | Guest's first name |
| lastName | Text | Guest's last name which will be set automatically with the name of the Host between parenthesis |
| identityType | Text | Is "Visitor" |
| pin | Text | Pin associated with the Guest |
| effectiveFrom | DateTime | The beginning date that a Guest's PIN is effective |
| effectiveTo | DateTime | The end date that a Guest's PIN is effective |
| suspended | Boolean | Whether the Guest is currently suspended |
| created | DateTime | The Guest's creation date |
| updated | DateTime | The Guest's update date |
| bleTwoFactorExempt | boolean | The user exempted from Ble two-factor authentication |
| customFields | CustomField\[\] | The custom field values for custom fields defined on the account |
| emails | Email\[\] | The Email objects associated with this User. |
| phoneNumbers | PhoneNumber\[\] | Array of PhoneNumber objects associated with this User. |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Guest-CreateAndAssignGuestUser-0_0_0-0)

```json
 {
    "id": 12422499,
    "firstName": "Guest 5 by admin",
    "lastName": "(host_name)",
    "identityType": "Visitor",
    "created": "2024-11-11T09:04:46Z",
    "updated": "2024-11-11T09:04:46Z",
    "pin": "175010",
    "effectiveFrom": "2024-11-11T10:18:50.549Z",
    "effectiveTo": "2024-11-30T15:18:00Z",
    "suspended": false,
    "bleTwoFactorExempt": false,
    "customFields": [],
    "emails": [\
        {\
            "id": 4431818,\
            "address": "cv@brivo.com",\
            "type": "work"\
        }\
    ],
    "phoneNumbers": []
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Guest-CreateAndAssignGuestUser-0_0_0-0)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Guest-CreateAndAssignGuestUser-0_0_0-1)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Guest-CreateAndAssignGuestUser-0_0_0-2)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Guest-CreateAndAssignGuestUser-0_0_0-3)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Guest-CreateAndAssignGuestUser-0_0_0-4)

```json
 HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
 {
    "message": "Provided groupId does not belong to the host's groups or it does not allow adding visitors.",
    "code": 400
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
   "message": "Provide groupIds for the visitor's access to doors",
   "code": 400
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
   "message": "Provide an email address where the visitor will receive the PIN credential",
   "code": 400
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

# Holidays

# Holidays - Holiday Listing

Retrieve a listing of Holidays.

- This action is only available to Brivo Account Config Tool Administrators
- Administrator must have access to a Site to retrieve holidays outside the Universal site

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/holidays
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | number | Listed results will display beginning from the offset value. |
| pageSize optional | number | The maximum number of records that will be returned for the call starting from the offset value.<br>Size range: `1-100` |
| filter optional | text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are:<br>- `name`<br>  - Filters based on holiday name<br>  - Allowed operators:<br>    - eq: includes any holiday with a name that contains the provided name value<br>- `site`<br>  - Filters based on site name. The site `"universal"` may be used to filter to only holidays that apply to all sites.<br>  - Allowed operators:<br>    - eq: includes any holiday with a site name that contains the provided name value<br>- `start`<br>  - Filters based on holiday start time<br>  - Allowed operators:<br>    - eq: includes any holiday with a start time of exactly the provided time value<br>    - gt: includes any holiday with a start time after the provided time value<br>- `end`<br>  - Filters based on holiday end time<br>  - Allowed operators:<br>    - eq: includes any holiday with an end time of exactly the provided time value<br>    - lt: includes any holiday with an end time before the provided time value |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | Holiday\[\] | Listing of Holiday Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |
| count | Number | Total count of results available for criteria |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Holidays-ListHolidays-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "data": [\
        {\
            "id": 12318,\
            "name": "New Year's Day",\
            "start": "2019-01-01T00:00:00",\
            "end": "2019-01-01T23:59:00",\
            "siteName": "Universal"\
        }\
    ],
    "offset": 0,
    "pageSize": 50,
    "count": 1
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Holidays-ListHolidays-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Holidays-ListHolidays-0_0_0-1)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

# Pass

# Pass - Get Mobile Pass

Retrieve a Brivo Mobile Pass. Brivo Mobile Pass allows you to open doors with your smartphone.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/pass
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| pass | Text | Brivo Mobile Pass |
| bleCredential | Text | The id of the ble credential retrieved |
| bleAuthTimeFrame | Number | The time frame that this will be enabled |
| enabled | Date | The date this pass was enabled |
| accountName | Text | The name of the account this pass belongs to |
| accountId | Number | The account id that this pass belongs to. |
| sites | Sites\[\] | Listing of sites this pass has access to<br>- `id` : The id used to reference the site<br>- `siteName` : The name associated with the site<br>- `address` : The address of the site<br>- `timeZone` : The timezone of the site<br>- `accessPoints` : A list of the access points that this pass will provide access to<br>- `preScreening` : An optional value for a site that will allow admins to provide prescreening questions to users using the mobile app before they enter a site<br>- `schedules` : A list of the schedules that this pass will be subject to |
| firstName | Text | User's first name |
| middleName | Text | User's middle name |
| lastName | Text | User's last name |
| UserImage | UserImage | An object containing information about the user's image |
| id | UserImage.id | The id associated with the image |
| uri | UserImage.uri | A url to view the user image that is active for 30 minutes |
| contentType | UserImage.contentType | The type of image or content |
| contentLength | UserImage.contentLength | The size of the image in bytes |
| created | UserImage.created | The date the image was created |
| enablePassTransfer | enablePassTransfer | The ENABLE\_PASS\_TRANSFER account setting property value, which by default is enabled for all accounts |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Pass-GetPass-0_0_0-0)

# Role - Create Role

Creates a role.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/roles
```

## Parameter

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| name | Text | The name of the role. |
| description | Text | The description of the role. |
| features | Feature\[\] | The features associated with the role. |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Role-CreateRole-0_0_0-0)

```json

{
    "name": "My Role",
    "description": "My Role Description",
    "features": [\
        {\
            "id": 14,\
            "permissionSet": "CUSTOM",\
            "permissions": [\
                18,\
                75\
            ]\
        },\
        {\
            "id": 15,\
            "permissionSet": "LIMITED"\
        },\
        {\
            "id": 19,\
            "permissionSet": "FULL"\
        },\
        {\
            "id": 21,\
            "permissionSet": "CUSTOM",\
            "permissions": [\
                12,\
                14\
            ]\
        },\
        {\
            "id": 26,\
            "permissionSet": "FULL"\
        },\
        {\
            "id": 28,\
            "permissionSet": "CUSTOM",\
            "permissions": [\
                32\
            ]\
        },\
        {\
            "id": 30,\
            "permissionSet": "FULL"\
        }\
    ]
}
```

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The ID of the created role. |
| name | Text | The name of the created role. |
| description | Text | The description of the created role. |
| roleType | Text | The type of the role. For created roles, the type is CUSTOM. |

# Role - Delete Role

Deletes a role.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/roles/:roleId
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| roleId | Number | (Required) The ID of the role to delete. |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Role-DeleteRole-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 204 No Content
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, Default or service roles cannot be deleted. |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 404 | Not Found, The requested role Id doesn't exist. |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Role-DeleteRole-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Role-DeleteRole-0_0_0-1)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Role-DeleteRole-0_0_0-2)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Role-DeleteRole-0_0_0-3)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Default or service roles cannot be deleted."
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "Access to the requested resource was denied"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "User unauthorized"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "The requested role Id doesn't exist."
}
```

```json
            "id": 32732,\
            "name": "Role 1",\
            "description": "My Role",\

        },\
        {\
            "id": 2,\
            "name": "Super Administrator",\
            "description": "Can edit other administrators",\
            "roleType": "DEFAULT"\
        }\

}
```

# Schedule

# Schedule - Create Schedule

Creates a schedule.

- This action is only available to Brivo Account Config Tool Administrators
- Assistant Administrators must have view and edit permissions to a site to create a site schedule, and will not be able to create Universal schedules.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/schedules/
```

## Parameter

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| name | Text | The schedule's name. Maximum 32 characters. |
| siteId optional | Number | The id of the site this schedule is associated to if a site schedule. Empty if not a site schedule. |
| enablingGroupId optional | Number | The id of the group that enables the schedule. Empty if not a group-enabled schedule. |
| gracePeriod optional | Number | Grace period for a group-enabled schedule. Empty if not a group-enabled schedule, otherwise valid values are 0-60. |
| scheduleBlocks | ScheduleBlock\[\] | The schedule blocks that define the overall schedule. Minimum one schedule block is needed and there's a maximum limit of 32 schedule time blocks per day. |
| scheduleExceptions optional | ScheduleException\[\] | The schedule exceptions that define the overall schedule exceptions in a schedule. There's a maximum limit of 16 schedule exceptions defined for a schedule. |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Schedule-Create_Schedule-0_0_0-0)

```json

{
    "name"              : "Now Standard 9 to 5",
    "siteId"            : 468795,
    "enablingGroupId"   : 84686,
    "gracePeriod"       : 10,
    "scheduleBlocks": {
        "monday"   : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "tuesday"  : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "wednesday": [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "thursday" : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "friday"   : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "saturday" : [{"start": "08:30", "end": "13:30"}],
        "sunday"   : [{"start": "08:30", "end": "13:30"}],
        "holiday"  : [{"start": "08:30", "end": "13:30"}]
    },
    "scheduleExceptions": [\
        {\
            "enabling"  : "DISABLE",\
            "start"     : "00:00",\
            "end"       : "23:59",\
            "recurrence": {\
                "type"       : "DAY_OF_MONTH",\
                "day"        : "WEDNESDAY",\
                "weekOfMonth": 2\
            }\
        },\
        {\
            "enabling"  : "ENABLE",\
            "start"     : "05:00",\
            "end"       : "09:00",\
            "recurrence": {\
                "type": "SINGULAR",\
                "date": "2022-03-19"\
            }\
        }\
    ]
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id associated with the schedule |
| name | Text | The schedule's name |
| siteId optional | Number | The id of the site this schedule is associated to if a site schedule. Empty if not a site schedule. |
| siteName optional | Text | The name of the site. For universal schedules, the name is "Universal" |
| enablingGroupId optional | Number | The id of the group that enables the schedule. Empty if not a group-enabled schedule. |
| enablingGroupName optional | Text | The name of the group. Empty if not a group-enabled schedule. |
| gracePeriod optional | Number | Grace period for a group-enabled schedule. Empty if not a group-enabled schedule. |
| scheduleBlocks | ScheduleBlock\[\] | The schedule blocks that define the overall schedule. |
| holidays | Holidays\[\] | The list of holidays in the schedule |
| scheduleExceptions | ScheduleException\[\] | The list of schedule exceptions in the schedule. |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Schedule-Create_Schedule-0_0_0-0)

```json

{
    "id"                : 498246,
    "name"              : "Now Standard 9 to 5",
    "siteId"            : 468795,
    "siteName"          : "Office",
    "enablingGroupId"   : 84686,
    "enablingGroupName" : "Desk Jockeys",
    "gracePeriod"       : 10,
    "scheduleBlocks": {
        "monday"   : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "tuesday"  : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "wednesday": [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "thursday" : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "friday"   : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "saturday" : [{"start": "08:30", "end": "13:30"}],
        "sunday"   : [{"start": "08:30", "end": "13:30"}],
        "holiday"  : [{"start": "08:30", "end": "13:30"}]
    },
    "holidays": [],
    "scheduleExceptions": [\
        {\
            "enabling"  : "DISABLE",\
            "start"     : "00:00",\
            "end"       : "23:59",\
            "recurrence": {\
                "type"       : "DAY_OF_MONTH",\
                "day"        : "WEDNESDAY",\
                "weekOfMonth": 2\
            }\
        },\
        {\
            "enabling"  : "ENABLE",\
            "start"     : "05:00",\
            "end"       : "09:00",\
            "recurrence": {\
                "type": "SINGULAR",\
                "date": "2022-03-19"\
            }\
        }\
    ]
}
```

# Schedule - Delete Schedule

Deletes the schedule associated with the provided id

- This action is only available to Brivo Account Config Tool Administrators
- Assistant Administrators must have view and edit permissions to a site to delete a site schedule, and will not be able to delete Universal schedules.
- Schedules that are associated with a group, device, and/or notification cannot be deleted until the associations are cleared
- 24x7 Schedule and (Always Access) Schedule are auto created for the account and cannot be deleted or edited

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/schedules/{scheduleId}
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| scheduleId | Number | The id associated with the schedule |

- [Success example](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Schedule-Delete_Schedule-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 204 No Content
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 404 | Not Found, the requested resource was not found. |
| 412 | Precondition Failed, the provided schedule has a dependent group access |

- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Schedule-Delete_Schedule-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Schedule-Delete_Schedule-0_0_0-1)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Schedule-Delete_Schedule-0_0_0-2)
- [412 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Schedule-Delete_Schedule-0_0_0-3)
- [412 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Schedule-Delete_Schedule-0_0_0-4)
- [412 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Schedule-Delete_Schedule-0_0_0-5)

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "This schedule cannot be edited or deleted"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "The requested resource was not found."
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 412 Precondition Failed
{
  "code"    : 412,
  "message" : "Schedule in use by: user group(s)"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 412 Precondition Failed
{
  "code"    : 412,
  "message" : "Schedule in use by: devices(s)"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 412 Precondition Failed
{
  "code"    : 412,
  "message" : "Schedule in use by: notification(s)"
}
```

# Schedule - Schedule Listing

Retrieve a listing of schedules

- This action is only available to Brivo Account Config Tool Administrators
- Administrator must have access to a Site to retrieve schedules outside the Universal site

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/schedules
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | number | Listed results will display beginning from the offset value. |
| pageSize optional | number | The maximum number of records that will be returned for the call starting from the offset value.<br>Size range: `1-100` |
| filter optional | text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are:<br>- `name`<br>  - Filters based on the schedule name<br>  - Allowed operators:<br>    - eq: includes any schedule with a name that contains the provided name value<br>- `enablingGroup`<br>  - Filters based on the enabling group name<br>  - Allowed operators:<br>    - eq: includes any schedule with the enabling group name that contains the provided name value<br>- `site`<br>  - Filters based on site name. The site “Universal” may be used to filter schedules that apply to all sites.<br>  - Allowed operators:<br>    - eq: includes any schedule with the site name that contains the provided name value<br>- `editable`<br>  - Filters based on if the schedule is editable<br>  - Allowed operators:<br>    - eq: includes any schedule with the editable attribute to identify if it is true or false |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | Schedule\[\] | Listing of Schedule Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |
| count | Number | Total count of results available for criteria |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Schedule-List_Schedules-0_0_0-0)

```json

{
    "data": [\
        {\
            "id": 44,\
            "name": "Office Schedule ABC",\
            "editable": true,\
            "siteName": "Universal"\
        },\
        {\
            "id": 64,\
            "name": "9 to 5 Office Schedule",\
            "editable": true,\
            "siteName": "Brivo East"\
        }\
    ],
    "offset": 0,
    "pageSize": 20,
    "count": 2
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request contains an invalid filter |

- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Schedule-List_Schedules-0_0_0-0)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Schedule-List_Schedules-0_0_0-1)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Schedule-List_Schedules-0_0_0-2)

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "Access to the requested resource was denied"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
    "message": "Invalid filter was provided",
    "code": 400
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
   "message": "Invalid filter operator",
    "code": 400
}
```

# Schedule - Schedule Retrieval

Retrieves a Schedule by the provided id value

- This action is only available to Brivo Account Config Tool Administrators
- Administrator must have access to a Site to retrieve schedules outside the Universal site

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/schedules/{scheduleId}
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| scheduleId | Number | The id associated with the schedule. |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id associated with the schedule |
| name | Text | The schedule's name |
| editable | Boolean | Returns false if it's a 24x7 default schedule. Otherwise, true. |
| siteId optional | Number | The id of the site this schedule is associated to if a site schedule. Empty if not a site schedule. |
| siteName optional | Text | The name of the site. For universal schedules, the name is "Universal" |
| enablingGroupId optional | Number | The id of the group that enables the schedule. Empty if not a group-enabled schedule. |
| enablingGroupName optional | Text | The name of the group. Empty if not a group-enabled schedule. |
| gracePeriod optional | Number | Grace period for a group-enabled schedule. Empty if not a group-enabled schedule, otherwise valid values are 0-60. |
| scheduleBlocks | ScheduleBlock\[\] | The schedule blocks that define the overall schedule. |
| holidays | Holidays\[\] | The list of holidays in the schedule |
| scheduleExceptions | ScheduleException\[\] | The list of schedule exceptions in the schedule. |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Schedule-Schedule_Retrieval-0_0_0-0)

```json

{
    "id"             : 498246,
    "name"           : "Now Standard 9 to 5",
    "editable"          : true,
    "siteId"            : 468795,
    "siteName"          : "Office",
    "enablingGroupId"   : 84686,
    "enablingGroupName" : "Desk Jockeys",
    "gracePeriod"       : 10,
    "scheduleBlocks": {
        "monday"   : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "tuesday"  : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "wednesday": [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "thursday" : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "friday"   : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "saturday" : [{"start": "08:30", "end": "13:30"}],
        "sunday"   : [{"start": "08:30", "end": "13:30"}],
        "holiday"  : [{"start": "08:30", "end": "13:30"}]
    },
    "scheduleExceptions": [{\
            "enabling"   : "ENABLE",\
            "start"      : "09:30",\
            "end"        : "10:30",\
            "recurrence" : {\
                "type" : "SINGULAR",\
                "date" : "2018-10-12"\
            }\
        },\
        {\
            "enabling"   : "DISABLE",\
            "start"      : "12:00",\
            "end"        : "17:00",\
            "recurrence" : {\
                "type"        : "DAY_OF_MONTH",\
                "day"         : "MONDAY",\
                "weekOfMonth" : 2\
            }\
        }\
    ],
    "holidays": [{\
        "name"   : "Halloween",\
        "start"  : "2018-10-31T00:00:00",\
        "end"    : "2018-10-31T23:59:59"\
    }]
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 404 | Not Found, the requested resource was not found. |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |

- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Schedule-Schedule_Retrieval-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Schedule-Schedule_Retrieval-0_0_0-1)

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "The requested resource was not found."
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "Access to the requested resource was denied"
}
```

# Schedule - Update Schedule

Updates a schedule.

- This action is only available to Brivo Account Config Tool Administrators
- Assistant Administrators must have view and edit permissions to a site to update a site schedule, and will not be able to update Universal schedules.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/schedules/{scheduleId}
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| scheduleId | Number | The id associated with the schedule. |

## Parameter

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| name | Text | The schedule's name. Maximum 32 characters. |
| enablingGroupId optional | Number | The id of the group that enables the schedule. Empty if not a group-enabled schedule. |
| gracePeriod optional | Number | Grace period for a group-enabled schedule. Empty if not a group-enabled schedule, otherwise valid values are 0-60. |
| scheduleBlocks | ScheduleBlock\[\] | The schedule blocks that define the overall schedule. Minimum one schedule block is needed and there's a maximum limit of 32 schedule time blocks per day. |
| scheduleExceptions optional | ScheduleException\[\] | The schedule exceptions that define the overall schedule exceptions in a schedule. There's a maximum limit of 16 schedule exceptions defined for a schedule. |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-Schedule-Update_Schedule-0_0_0-0)

```json

{
    "name"           : "Now Standard 9 to 5",
    "enablingGroupId"   : 84686,
    "gracePeriod"       : 10,
    "scheduleBlocks": {
        "monday"   : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "tuesday"  : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "wednesday": [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "thursday" : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "friday"   : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "saturday" : [{"start": "08:30", "end": "13:30"}],
        "sunday"   : [{"start": "08:30", "end": "13:30"}],
        "holiday"  : [{"start": "08:30", "end": "13:30"}]
    },
    "scheduleExceptions": [\
        {\
            "enabling"  : "DISABLE",\
            "start"     : "00:00",\
            "end"       : "23:59",\
            "recurrence": {\
                "type"       : "DAY_OF_MONTH",\
                "day"        : "WEDNESDAY",\
                "weekOfMonth": 2\
            }\
        },\
        {\
            "enabling"  : "ENABLE",\
            "start"     : "05:00",\
            "end"       : "09:00",\
            "recurrence": {\
                "type": "SINGULAR",\
                "date": "2022-03-19"\
            }\
        }\
    ]
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id associated with the schedule |
| name | Text | The schedule's name |
| siteId optional | Number | The id of the site this schedule is associated to if a site schedule. Empty if not a site schedule. |
| siteName optional | Text | The name of the site. For universal schedules, the name is "Universal" |
| enablingGroupId optional | Number | The id of the group that enables the schedule. Empty if not a group-enabled schedule. |
| enablingGroupName optional | Text | The name of the group. Empty if not a group-enabled schedule. |
| gracePeriod optional | Number | Grace period for a group-enabled schedule. Empty if not a group-enabled schedule. |
| scheduleBlocks | ScheduleBlock\[\] | The schedule blocks that define the overall schedule. |
| scheduleExceptions | ScheduleException\[\] | The list of schedule exceptions in the schedule. |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Schedule-Update_Schedule-0_0_0-0)

```json

{
    "id"             : 498246,
    "name"           : "Now Standard 9 to 5",

    "siteName"          : "Office",

    "enablingGroupName" : "Desk Jockeys",
    "gracePeriod"       : 10,
    "scheduleBlocks": {
        "monday"   : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "tuesday"  : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "wednesday": [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "thursday" : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "friday"   : [{"start": "09:00", "end": "17:00"}],
        "saturday" : [{"start": "08:30", "end": "13:30"}],
        "sunday"   : [{"start": "08:30", "end": "13:30"}],

                "day"        : "WEDNESDAY",\
                "weekOfMonth": 2\
            }\
        },\

            "end"       : "09:00",\
            "recurrence": {\
                "type": "SINGULAR",\
```

# Site - Gets proximity information for a Site

- This action is only available to Brivo Account Config Tool Administrators


## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| siteId | number | id associated with the site |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The Site's id value |
| siteName | Text | The Site's name |
| proximity | Proximity | Proximity point of the site |
| wifi | Wifi\[\] | A list of WiFi points of the site |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Site-RetrieveProximityBySite-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "id": 196098,
    "siteName": "1_SaltoTestSite",
    "proximity": {
              "wifi": [\
                         {\
                             "ssid": "nonwifi"\
                         },\
                         {\
                             "ssid": "wifi1"\
                         },\
                         {\
                             "ssid": "wifi2"\
                         }\
                     ]
                 }
}
```

| --- | --- |

```json

{
```
```json
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

```json
                         }\

                       "wifi" : [\

   }\
```

# Site - Site Listing

Retrieve a listing of sites that are viewable to the caller

- This action is only available to Brivo Account Config Tool and Card Holders

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/sites
```

- [Filter-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#examples-Site-ListSites-0_0_0-0)

```text
/sites?filter=name__eq:Site+1
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | number | Listed results will display beginning from the offset value. |
| pageSize optional | number | The maximum number of records that will be returned for the call starting from the offset value.<br>Size range: `1-100` |
| filter optional | text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are<br>- `name`<br>  - Filters based on a site name<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any sites with a name that contains the provided name value |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | Site\[\] | Listing of Site Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |
| count | Number | Total count of results available for criteria |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Site-ListSites-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "data": [\
   {\
    "id"   : 111,\
    "siteName" : "Site 1"\
    },\
    {\
    "id"   : 222,\
     "siteName" : "Site 2"\
    }\
  ],
  "offset": 0,
  "pageSize": 20,
  "count": 2
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, Invalid listing criteria specified |

- [Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-Site-ListSites-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
    "code"    : 400,
    "message" : "Invalid listing criteria provided"
}
```

# Site - Site Retrieval

```html

```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| siteId | number | id associated with the site |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The Site's id value |
| siteName | Text | The Site's name |
| timeZone | TimeZone | The Site's configured timezone |
| address | Address | Street address of the returned Site |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-Site-RetrieveSite-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "id"        : 111,
    "siteName"  : "Site 1",
    "timeZone"  : "US/Eastern",
    "address"   : {
                    "streetAddress1"     : "Text",
                    "streetAddress2"     : "Text",
                    "city"               : "Text",
                    "state"              : "Text",
                    "postalCode"         : "Text",
                    "country"            : "Text",
                    "telephoneNumber"    : "Text",
                    "telephoneExtension" : "Text"
                  }
}
```

| --- | --- |

```json
{
    "code"    : 404,
    "message" : "Site not found"
```
```json
}
```

# User

# User - Assign Credential and Dates

Assigns a Credential to a User and sets the effective date range that the credential is valid for use.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/users/{userId}/credentials/{credentialId}
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| userId | number | id associated with the user |
| credentialId | number | id associated with the credential |

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| EffectiveDateRange optional | json | Date range where a user's credential is enabled for use. The request body may consist of<br>- `effectiveFrom`<br>  - The starting time when a user's credential will begin to be valid.<br>- `effectiveTo`<br>  - The ending time, after which a user's credential will no longer be valid.<br>Both of the values are optional.<br>If no values are specified and the credential is already assigned to the user, no changes will be made.<br>If no values are specified and the credential is not currently assigned to the user, the effectiveFrom date will default to the current time and the effectiveTo will be left empty.<br>If only an effectiveTo date is provided, the effectiveFrom will be set to the existing effectiveFrom or to the current time if the credential was not previously assigned to the user. |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-User-UserAssignCredential-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "effectiveFrom" : "2015-06-01T17:00:00Z",
  "effectiveTo"   : "2016-07-31T17:00:00Z"
}
```

- [Successful Response](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-User-UserAssignCredential-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 204 No Content
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | The specified Credential was not valid |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 404 | Not Found, the specified user was not found |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-UserAssignCredential-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-UserAssignCredential-0_0_0-1)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-UserAssignCredential-0_0_0-2)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Credential not valid"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "User not found"
}
```

# User - Create new user

Create a new user

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/users
```

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| firstName | Text | User's first name |
| middleName optional | Text | User's middle name |
| lastName | Text | User's last name |
| externalId optional | Text | An ID defined by clients which is guaranteed to be unique within the clients Brivo Access account. This is often used to store a surrogate key from a clients own Identity Management platform which can reliably link two users. An example would be to use a Users objectGUID attribute from Active Directory which is also guaranteed to be unique |
| pin optional | Text | Pin associated with the user |
| effectiveFrom optional | DateTime | The beginning date that a user's PIN is valid for use. |
| effectiveTo optional | DateTime | The end date that a user's PIN is valid for use. |
| bleTwoFactorExempt optional | boolean | is the user exempted from Ble two-factor authentication |
| emails optional | Email\[\] | Array of Email objects associated with this User. Email has address {Text} and type {Text}. |
| phoneNumbers optional | PhoneNumber\[\] | Array of PhoneNumber objects associated with this User. PhoneNumber has number {Text} and type {Text}. |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-User-CreateUser-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "firstName"    : "Peter",
  "middleName"   : "Jason",
  "lastName"     : "Quill",
  "externalId"   : "Star Lord",
  "pin"          : "5678",
  "effectiveFrom": "2015-04-14T18:17:49Z",
  "effectiveTo"  : "2020-12-31T23:59:59Z",
  "bleTwoFactorExempt"     : true,
  "emails"    : [{\
                    "address": "peter.quill@brivo.com",\
                    "type": "home"\
                    },\
                    {\
                    "address": "pquill7777@gmail.com",\
                    "type": "work"\
                    }],
  "phoneNumbers"    : [{\
                    "number": "(541) 754-3010",\
                    "type": "home"\
                    },\
                    {\
                    "number": "+1-541-754-3010",\
                    "type": "work"\
                    },\
                    {\
                    "number": "+49-89-636-48018",\
                    "type": "other"\
                    }]
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id associated with the user |
| externalId | Text | An alternate id specified by the account administrators |
| firstName | Text | User's first name |
| middleName | Text | User's middle name |
| lastName | Text | User's last name |
| pin | Text | Pin associated with the user |
| effectiveFrom | DateTime | The beginning date that a user's PIN is effective |
| effectiveTo | DateTime | The end date that a user's PIN is effective |
| suspended | Boolean | Whether the user is currently suspended |
| created | DateTime | The user's creation date |
| updated | DateTime | The user's update date |
| bleTwoFactorExempt | boolean | is the user exempted from Ble two-factor authentication |
| UserImage | UserImage | An object containing information about the user's image |
| id | UserImage.id | The id associated with the image |
| uri | UserImage.uri | A url to view the user image that is active for 30 minutes |
| customFields | CustomField\[\] | The custom field values for custom fields defined on the account |
| emails | Email\[\] | The Email objects associated with this User. |
| phoneNumbers | PhoneNumber\[\] | Array of PhoneNumber objects associated with this User. |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-User-CreateUser-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
 "id"           : 442211,
 "externalId"   : "Star Lord",
 "firstName"    : "Peter",
 "middleName"   : "Jason",
 "lastName"     : "Quill",
 "pin"          : "5678",
 "effectiveFrom": "2015-04-14T18:17:49Z",
 "effectiveTo"  : "2020-12-31T23:59:59Z",
 "suspended"    : false,
 "created":     : "2010-06-15T04:00:00Z",
 "updated":     : "2018-03-14T04:00:00Z",
 "bleTwoFactorExempt"    :true,
 "userImage"     : [{\
                    "id" : 5678,\
                    "uri" : "http://aws.my.image.uri.com.net.stuff"\
                  }],
 "customFields" : [{\
                    "id"        : 222,\
                    "fieldType" : "TEXT",\
                    "fieldName" : "species",\
                    "value"     : "human"\
                   },\
                   {\
                    "id"        : 233,\
                    "fieldType" : "DATE",\
                    "fieldName" : "Birth Date",\
                    "value"     : "02/04/1962"\
                   }],
 "emails"    : [{\
                   "address": "peter.quill@brivo.com",\
                   "type": "home"\
                   },\
                   {\
                   "address": "pquill7777@gmail.com",\
                   "type": "work"\
                   }],
 "phoneNumbers"    : [{\
                   "number": "(541) 754-3010",\
                   "type": "home"\
                   },\
                   {\
                   "number": "+1-541-754-3010",\
                   "type": "work"\
                   },\
                   {\
                   "number": "+49-89-636-48018",\
                   "type": "other"\
                   }]
 }
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-CreateUser-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-CreateUser-0_0_0-1)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
```

- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-Delete_User-0_0_0-1)

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "User not found"
```
```json
}
```

# User - List Users

Retrieve a listing of Users

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/users
```

## Query String

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| offset optional | number | Listed results will display beginning from the offset value. |
| pageSize optional | number | The maximum number of records that will be returned for the call starting from the offset value.<br>Size range: `1-100` |
| filter optional | text | Filters follow the common [filter format](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#filters) for the api.<br>Available filter criteria are<br>- `id`<br>  <br>  - Filters based on the user id.<br>  - Multiple values can be comma separated<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any user from the user ids provided<br>    - ne: excludes any user from the user ids provided<br>- `firstname`<br>  <br>  - Filters based on a user's first name<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any user with a first name that contains the provided firstname value<br>- `lastname`<br>  <br>  - Filters based on a user's last name<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any user with a last name that contains the provided lastname value<br>- `user_status`<br>  <br>  - Filters based on a user's status<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: includes any user that falls under the corresponding status<br>  - Allowed user\_status values<br>    - active: returns users who have at least one active credential with an effective date range that would include the current date, and be assigned to at least one group.<br>    - unaffiliated: returns the listing of users who are not assigned to a group.<br>    - suspended: returns the listing of suspended users<br>    - deleted (deprecated): it is not supported anymore so it returns an empty result<br>- `cf_{customFieldId}`<br>  <br>  - Filters based on a specified custom field id<br>    - For example, a custom field with an id=1234 a filter would look like `cf_1234__eq:searchValue`<br>  - Allowed operators<br>    - eq: Custom field types are taken into account during filtering.<br>      - DATE values must be provided in the custom\_field date pattern of the definition<br>      - NUMBER values will be matched on any exact field value<br>      - TEXT values will return any field value that contains the requested filter value<br>    - exact: Custom field types are taken into account during filtering.<br>      - DATE values must be provided in the custom\_field date pattern of the definition<br>      - NUMBER values will be matched on any exact field value<br>      - TEXT values will return any field value that exactly matches the requested filter value |

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data | User\[\] | Listing of User Objects |
| offset | Number | Offset the listing was run with |
| pageSize | Number | Page Size the listing was run with |
| count | Number | Total count of results available for criteria |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-User-ListUsers-0_0_0-0)

```json
 {
    "data": [\
        {\
            "id": 8784984,\
            "firstName": "John",\
            "lastName": "Doe",\
            "created": "2023-04-11T01:35:12Z",\
            "updated": "2024-11-25T07:08:24Z",\
            "suspended": false,\
            "bleTwoFactorExempt": false,\
            "customFields": [],\
            "emails": [\
                {\
                    "address": "test@test.com",\
                    "type": "Work"\
                },\
                {\
                    "address": "hometest@test.com",\
                    "type": "Home"\
                }\
            ],\
            "phoneNumbers": [\
                {\
                    "type": "Work",\
                    "number": "1234567890"\
                },\
                {\
                    "type": "Home",\
                    "number": "9876543210"\
                }\
            ]\
        }\
    ],
    "offset": 0,
    "pageSize": 20,
    "count": 1
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-ListUsers-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

# User - Patch user

Patch a user with the specified userId value.

Optional fields that are omitted from the request body will remain unchanged.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/users/{userId}
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| userId | Number | The id associated with the user |

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| firstName optional | Text | User's first name |
| middleName optional | Text | User's middle name |
| lastName optional | Text | User's last name |
| externalId optional | Text | An ID defined by clients which is guaranteed to be unique within the clients Brivo Access account. This is often used to store a surrogate key from a clients own Identity Management platform which can reliably link two users. An example would be to use a Users objectGUID attribute from Active Directory which is also guaranteed to be unique |
| pin optional | Text | Pin associated with the user |
| effectiveFrom optional | DateTime | The beginning date that a user's PIN is valid for use. |
| effectiveTo optional | DateTime | The end date that a user's PIN is valid for use. |
| bleTwoFactorExempt optional | boolean | is the user exempted from Ble two-factor authentication |
| emails optional | Email\[\] | Array of Email objects associated with this User. Email has address {Text} and type {Text}. |
| phoneNumbers optional | PhoneNumber\[\] | Array of PhoneNumber objects associated with this User. PhoneNumber has number {Text} and type {Text}. |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-User-PatchUser-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "firstName"    : "Changed Peter",
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id associated with the user |
| externalId | Text | An alternate id specified by the account administrators |
| firstName | Text | User's first name |
| middleName | Text | User's middle name |
| lastName | Text | User's last name |
| pin | Text | Pin associated with the user |
| effectiveFrom | DateTime | The beginning date that a user's PIN is effective |
| effectiveTo | DateTime | The end date that a user's PIN is effective |
| suspended | Boolean | Whether the user is currently suspended |
| created | DateTime | The user's creation date |
| updated | DateTime | The user's update date |
| bleTwoFactorExempt | boolean | is the user exempted from Ble two-factor authentication |
| UserImage | UserImage | An object containing information about the user's image |
| id | UserImage.id | The id associated with the image |
| uri | UserImage.uri | A url to view the user image that is active for 30 minutes |
| customFields | CustomField\[\] | The custom field values for custom fields defined on the account |
| emails | Email\[\] | The Email objects associated with this User. |
| phoneNumbers | PhoneNumber\[\] | Array of PhoneNumber objects associated with this User. |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-User-PatchUser-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
 "id"           : 442211,
 "externalId"   : "Star Lord",
 "firstName"    : "Changed Peter",
 "middleName"   : "Jason",
 "lastName"     : "Quill",
 "pin"          : "5678",
 "effectiveFrom": "2015-04-14T18:17:49Z",
 "effectiveTo"  : "2020-12-31T23:59:59Z",
 "suspended"    : false,
 "created":     : "2010-06-15T04:00:00Z",
 "updated":     : "2018-03-14T04:00:00Z",
 "bleTwoFactorExempt"    :true,
 "userImage"     : [{\
                    "id" : 5678,\
                    "uri" : "http://aws.my.image.uri.com.net.stuff"\
                  }],
 "customFields" : [{\
                    "id"        : 222,\
                    "fieldType" : "TEXT",\
                    "fieldName" : "species",\
                    "value"     : "human"\
                   },\
                   {\
                    "id"        : 233,\
                    "fieldType" : "DATE",\
                    "fieldName" : "Birth Date",\
                    "value"     : "02/04/1962"\
                   }],
 "emails"    : [{\
                   "address": "peter.quill@brivo.com",\
                   "type": "home"\
                   },\
                   {\
                   "address": "pquill7777@gmail.com",\
                   "type": "work"\
                   }],
 "phoneNumbers"    : [{\
                   "number": "(541) 754-3010",\
                   "type": "home"\
                   },\
                   {\
                   "number": "+1-541-754-3010",\
                   "type": "work"\
                   },\
                   {\
                   "number": "+49-89-636-48018",\
                   "type": "other"\
                   }]
 }
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 404 | Not Found, the specified user was not found |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-PatchUser-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-PatchUser-0_0_0-1)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-PatchUser-0_0_0-2)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "User not found"
}
```
