```json
 "emails"    : [{\
                   "address": "peter.quill@brivo.com",\
                   "type": "home"\
                   },\
                   {\
                   "address": "pquill7777@gmail.com",\
                   "type": "work"\
                   }],
 "phoneNumbers"    : [{\
                   "number": "(541) 754-3010",\
                   "type": "home"\
                   },\
                   {\
                   "number": "+1-541-754-3010",\
                   "type": "work"\
                   },\
                   {\
                   "number": "+49-89-636-48018",\
                   "type": "other"\
                   }]
 }
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 404 | Not Found, the specified user was not found |

- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-RetrieveUser-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "User not found"
}
```

# User - Toggle suspended status

Updates the suspended status of a user specified by the provided userId to the suspended status in the request body

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/users/{userId}/suspended
```

## Request body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| suspended | boolean | The suspended status to update the user to |

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| userId | Number | The id associated with the user |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-User-ToggleSuspendedStatus-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "suspended" : false
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | number | The id associated with the user |
| suspended | boolean | The current suspended status of the associated user |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-User-ToggleSuspendedStatus-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "id"        : 12345,
  "suspended" : false
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 404 | Not Found, the specified user was not found |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-ToggleSuspendedStatus-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-ToggleSuspendedStatus-0_0_0-1)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-ToggleSuspendedStatus-0_0_0-2)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "User not found"
}
```

# User - Update Custom Field Value

Updates the value of the specified custom field id.

The value must be valid for the type definition of the custom field.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/users/{userId}/custom-fields/{customFieldId}
```

## RequestBody

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| value | Text | The new custom field value.<br>This value will be validated against the custom field's type definition. A value that will not map to the specified custom field's type will return a 400 Bad Request response. |

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| userId | Number | The id associated with the user |
| customFieldId | Number | The id associated with the custom field |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-User-UpdateCustomField-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "value" : "Engineering"
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The ID associated with the custom field |
| fieldType | Text | Type of value allowed in the custom field. Allowed values are:<br>- TEXT<br>- NUMBER<br>- DATE |
| fieldName | Text | Display name of the custom field |
| value | Text | The text representation of the custom field's value |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-User-UpdateCustomField-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
 "id"       : 54321,
 "fieldType": "TEXT",
 "fieldName": "Department",
 "value"    : "Engineering"
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 404 | Not Found, the specified user was not found |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-UpdateCustomField-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-UpdateCustomField-0_0_0-1)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-UpdateCustomField-0_0_0-2)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "User not found"
}
```

# User - Update user

Update a user with the specified userId value.

Optional fields which are not included in the request body will have any existing value removed.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/users/{userId}
```

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| userId | Number | The id associated with the user |

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| firstName | Text | User's first name |
| middleName optional | Text | User's middle name |
| lastName | Text | User's last name |
| externalId optional | Text | An ID defined by clients which is guaranteed to be unique within the clients Brivo Access account. This is often used to store a surrogate key from a clients own Identity Management platform which can reliably link two users. An example would be to use a Users objectGUID attribute from Active Directory which is also guaranteed to be unique |
| pin optional | Text | Pin associated with the user |
| effectiveFrom optional | DateTime | The beginning date that a user's PIN is valid for use. |
| effectiveTo optional | DateTime | The end date that a user's PIN is valid for use. |
| bleTwoFactorExempt optional | boolean | is the user exempted from Ble two-factor authentication |
| emails optional | Email\[\] | Array of Email objects associated with this User. Email has address {Text} and type {Text}. |
| phoneNumbers optional | PhoneNumber\[\] | Array of PhoneNumber objects associated with this User. PhoneNumber has number {Text} and type {Text}. |

- [Request-Body-Example:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-User-UpdateUser-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
  "firstName"    : "Peter",
  "middleName"   : "Jason",
  "lastName"     : "Quill",
  "externalId"   : "Star Lord",
  "pin"          : "5678",
  "effectiveFrom": "2015-04-14T18:17:49Z",
  "effectiveTo"  : "2020-12-31T23:59:59Z",
  "bleTwoFactorExempt"     : true,
  "emails"    : [{\
                    "address": "peter.quill@brivo.com",\
                    "type": "home"\
                    },\
                    {\
                    "address": "pquill7777@gmail.com",\
                    "type": "work"\
                    }],
  "phoneNumbers"    : [{\
                    "number": "(541) 754-3010",\
                    "type": "home"\
                    },\
                    {\
                    "number": "+1-541-754-3010",\
                    "type": "work"\
                    },\
                    {\
                    "number": "+49-89-636-48018",\
                    "type": "other"\
                    }]
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| id | Number | The id associated with the user |
| externalId | Text | An alternate id specified by the account administrators |
| firstName | Text | User's first name |
| middleName | Text | User's middle name |
| lastName | Text | User's last name |
| pin | Text | Pin associated with the user |
| effectiveFrom | DateTime | The beginning date that a user's PIN is effective |
| effectiveTo | DateTime | The end date that a user's PIN is effective |
| suspended | Boolean | Whether the user is currently suspended |
| created | DateTime | The user's creation date |
| updated | DateTime | The user's update date |
| bleTwoFactorExempt | boolean | is the user exempted from Ble two-factor authentication |
| UserImage | UserImage | An object containing information about the user's image |
| id | UserImage.id | The id associated with the image |
| uri | UserImage.uri | A url to view the user image that is active for 30 minutes |
| customFields | CustomField\[\] | The custom field values for custom fields defined on the account |
| emails | Email\[\] | The Email objects associated with this User. |
| phoneNumbers | PhoneNumber\[\] | Array of PhoneNumber objects associated with this User. |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-User-UpdateUser-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
 "id"           : 442211,
 "externalId"   : "Star Lord",
 "firstName"    : "Peter",
 "middleName"   : "Jason",
 "lastName"     : "Quill",
 "pin"          : "5678",
 "effectiveFrom": "2015-04-14T18:17:49Z",
 "effectiveTo"  : "2020-12-31T23:59:59Z",
 "suspended"    : false,
 "created":     : "2010-06-15T04:00:00Z",
 "updated":     : "2018-03-14T04:00:00Z",
 "bleTwoFactorExempt"    :true,
 "userImage"     : [{\
                    "id" : 5678,\
                    "uri" : "http://aws.my.image.uri.com.net.stuff"\
                  }],
 "customFields" : [{\
                    "id"        : 222,\
                    "fieldType" : "TEXT",\
                    "fieldName" : "species",\
                    "value"     : "human"\
                   },\
                   {\
                    "id"        : 233,\
                    "fieldType" : "DATE",\
                    "fieldName" : "Birth Date",\
                    "value"     : "02/04/1962"\
                   }],
 "emails"    : [{\
                   "address": "peter.quill@brivo.com",\
                   "type": "home"\
                   },\
                   {\
                   "address": "pquill7777@gmail.com",\
                   "type": "work"\
                   }],
 "phoneNumbers"    : [{\
                   "number": "(541) 754-3010",\
                   "type": "home"\
                   },\
                   {\
                   "number": "+1-541-754-3010",\
                   "type": "work"\
                   },\
                   {\
                   "number": "+49-89-636-48018",\
                   "type": "other"\
                   }]
 }
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |
| 404 | Not Found, the specified user was not found |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-UpdateUser-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-UpdateUser-0_0_0-1)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-UpdateUser-0_0_0-2)

```json
  "code"    : 400,

}
```

```json
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
```

# User - Update user's group memberships

Simultaneously add or remove user's group memberships, or do both at once. Groups to be added will be skipped if the user is already a member, and groups to be removed will be skipped if the user is not a member. A user can be a member of at most 16 groups. If the user's total number of groups would exceed 16 after all removals and additions are made, it is considered an error and no action will be taken. Note that this could also include groups which the administrator does not have permission to view. Returns the updated list of user's group memberships.

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/users/{id}/groups
```

## Request Body

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| addGroups | Number\[\] | A list of group IDs to add the user to. Optional. |

## RequestBody

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| removeGroups | Number\[\] | A list of group IDs to remove the user from. Optional. |

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| userId | Number | The id associated with the user |

- [AddOnly-Example](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-User-UpdateUsersGroups-0_0_0-0)
- [RemoveOnly-Example](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-User-UpdateUsersGroups-0_0_0-1)
- [AddAndRemove-Example](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#parameter-examples-User-UpdateUsersGroups-0_0_0-2)

```json
{
    "addGroups": [76123, 16632]
}
```

```json
{
    "removeGroups": [76336]
}
```

```json
{
    "addGroups": [76123, 16632],
    "removeGroups": [76336]
}
```

## Success 200

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| data: | Group\[\] | Listing of Group objects |
| count | Number | Total number of groups of which the user is a member |

- [Success-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-User-UpdateUsersGroups-0_0_0-0)

```json
{
    "count": 2,
    "data": [\
        {\
            "id": 76123,\
            "name": "Managers"\
        },\
        {\
            "id": 16632,\
            "name": "First Floor"\
        }\
    ]
}
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 404 | Not Found, the specified user was not found |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |

- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-UpdateUsersGroups-0_0_0-0)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-UpdateUsersGroups-0_0_0-1)
- [404 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-UpdateUsersGroups-0_0_0-2)
- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-UpdateUsersGroups-0_0_0-3)

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "User not found"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "Group not found/ Unknown Group"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found
{
  "code"    : 404,
  "message" : "Group not found"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
  "code"    : 400,
  "message" : "Invalid criteria provided"
}
```

# User - Upload user photo

Upload a photo to a user

```html
https://api.brivo.com/v1/api/users/{userId}/photo
```

## MultipartFile

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| file | File | The user photo file with format of png, jpg, jpeg or gif |

## Path Parameters

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| userId | Number | The id associated with the user |

- [Successful Response](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#success-examples-User-UploadUserPhoto-0_0_0-0)

```json
HTTP/1.1 204 No Content
```

## Error code

| Field | Description |
| --- | --- |
| 400 | Bad Request, the provided request criteria are not valid |
| 403 | Forbidden, the attempted action is forbidden |

- [400 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-UploadUserPhoto-0_0_0-0)
- [403 Error-Response:](https://apidocs.brivo.com/#error-examples-User-UploadUserPhoto-0_0_0-1)

```json
HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
{
   "code"    : 400,
   "message" : "Content-type header of multipart/form-data must be set and uploaded file is added"
}
```

```json
HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden
{
  "code"    : 403,
  "message" : "You are not allowed to perform that action"
}
```
